Record of Antiquities Excavated in Southern Lu - Teng County Begins Work - Speculation on Being the Territory of the Small Zhu State 94

Teng County Correspondence. The Academia Sinica and the Shandong Institute of Ancient Relics Research have jointly excavated ancient relics in the three counties of Zuo, Teng, and Yi in Southern Lu, in order to study and verify ancient history, culture, and art. The responsible persons are Dong Zuobin from the Academia Sinica and Wang Xiantang from the Shandong Institute. Dong and his team arrived in Teng on the 19th and went to Anshang on the 20th. All personnel are staying in Anshang Village. Anshang Village is thirty li southeast of Teng County. Those working at the site every day include Qi Yanpei, Mou Xiangnong (Deputy Director of the Provincial Library), Pan Ke, Wang Xiang, and Li Lanfang. There is also a squad of soldiers from the Fourth Route Militia, led by

Page 8

Sun Yizhai, the second platoon leader of the Teng County Brigade, for protection. According to Dong Zuobin, the area currently being excavated is commonly called Gutuiding (Mound Top). To the east, the high mountain is Gutai Mountain, and to the west, it's called Tao Mountain. It's likely named so because of its elevated terrain. According to historical records, it should be the territory of the Small Zhu State, which is also the place where Zhou Dynasty bronzes were unearthed this spring. The excavation area covers 30 meters from east to west and 80 meters from north to south, with a total of six pits opened, each one meter wide and ten meters long from east to west. If necessary, the excavation will be expanded. Work began on the 24th. To facilitate the work, each person is in charge of one pit, and twenty workers are hired to dig and open the pits, from south to north. Li Fanglan is responsible for monitoring and inspecting the items excavated from the first pit; Wang Xiang for the second pit; myself (Dong speaking) for the third pit; Qi Yanpei for the fourth pit; Mou Xiangnong for the fifth pit; and Pan Ke for the sixth pit. All items excavated from each pit, such as pottery, bone fragments, and shells, are recorded for their location and depth from the ground, separately preserved and wrapped, and then cleaned before being identified. Most of the items found on the 24th were pottery shards, a deer antler about half a meter long, a conch shell, and a bone arrowhead. In the eastern section of the third pit, a human skeleton was found. At the western end, a round hole with a diameter of about six inches was discovered, filled with a large amount of loose, gray-black soil. I believe that this place was originally a residence and later became a base before being transformed into farmland. The red soil found in the second pit is likely the location of a stove. The round hole in the third pit, filled with ash, is the stove's chimney. The large number of conch shells and clam shells were a favorite food of the people who lived here. These items are also abundant at Chengziya and the Yin Ruins in Anyang. The bone arrowhead was one of the weapons used at the time, because before the Warring States period, during the Shang and Zhou dynasties, metal was scarce, and stone and bone artifacts were numerous. It was not until the late Zhou Dynasty, during the Spring and Autumn and Warring States periods, that bronze became prevalent, and arrowheads were made of bronze. Based on this, the age of the site can undoubtedly be determined to be from the Spring and Autumn and Warring States periods. As for the human bones, because they were very close to the surface and the bone structure was disarranged and incomplete, they were likely the remains of a reburial. It is unfortunate that there are no epitaphs or steles to provide evidence for research. In the future, all the bones will be sent to Beiping to the paleontology technician Mr. Yang Zhongjian to study the ancient human races and ancient animals. The entire project is still in its initial stages. After the excavation is complete, all the information about this place, where the houses were, where the kitchens were, the doors and courtyards, and the entire layout of the courtyard, will reveal the lives of the ancient people, their architectural art, and further extrapolate to history and culture. Its contribution will be far from superficial. Dong also said that they get up at 6:00 am every day, have breakfast at 10:00 am, start work at 8:00 am, rest and have lunch at 12:00 pm, continue working at 1:00 pm, and stop working at 5:00 pm for dinner. Each person makes a brief report on the day's work. The total working time is eight hours per day. In addition, twenty people are hired to dig pits. Their wages are 30 cents of silver per person per day. The work at this site will be completed in about thirty days. The depth of each pit, unless there is a special discovery, will be dug to the yellow soil layer. The work in Zou and Yi counties is expected to complete all the survey procedures in Zou County this year. The excavation period will be carried out simultaneously with Yi County next spring. The construction in Teng County will definitely be completed within the year.

On the 25th, the excavation reached the 15th pit, and bone awls, stone knife fragments, and stone axe fragments were found. There were also many holes in each pit. In addition to broken pottery shards, there were also bronze arrowheads, which were already decayed and only about an inch long, with a square head and a biased prismatic shape.

On the 26th, the 17th pit was continued, which is the place where the local people unearthed Zhou Dynasty bronzes this spring. On that day, Dong also told the reporter that the working area north of Anshang Village, we will tentatively call it the "Anshang Site". The locals call it Gutuiding (Mound Top) because the gray soil is higher than the ground and forms a mound. We have only been working for three days, and our observations are still very rough. Generally speaking: (1) The scope of the site is the same as previously mentioned; (2) The search for the site, the result of opening seventeen pits in three days, can be inferred: (A) The ground level at that time was about 70 to 80 cm below the current ground level; (B) There were small round pits with a diameter of six or seven inches and a depth of four or five inches on the ground at that time, filled with black ash and charcoal, which resembled stoves; (C) There were large round pits with a diameter of four or five meters and a depth of more than one meter next to the stoves. It remains to be studied whether these round pits were used for living or storage; (D) At a depth of 20 to 30 cm below the cultivated soil, a soil platform resembling a house foundation was discovered; (3) The collection of artifacts. The artifacts are mostly found in the ash layer, scattered and discarded, with no order to be found. Pottery shards are the most numerous, but they are also too fragmented to form complete vessels. The artifacts unearthed today can be divided into six categories: (A) Pottery: Tripod legs are quite numerous. There are also fragments of Dou, Lei, Zun, and Yi vessels. The most noteworthy is the black pottery shards that are similar to those produced at Chengziya, which are also found here, but the shape is thicker and coarser, not as refined as those produced at Chengziya, and the patterns are simpler, without text, which is their unique feature; (B) Bone artifacts: There are bone arrowheads, bone awls, and flat needles with holes; (C) Stone artifacts: Stone arrowheads, stone sickles with holes, stone chisels, and stone knives are particularly noteworthy. The shapes are all similar to those unearthed at the Yin Ruins; (D) Shell artifacts: There are shell sickles and knives with serrated edges, very similar to those produced by the lower-layer black pottery culture of Chengziya; (E) Bronze artifacts: Only bronze arrowheads and bronze scraps are seen; (F) Animal bones are not very numerous, but there are also deer antlers and wild boar teeth.

On the afternoon of the 27th, traces of ancient tombs were discovered underground at the "Anshang Site". According to Dong's determination, it was briefly stated that on the afternoon of the 27th, while continuing to excavate the 17th pit, a ditch dug by the Chen Shangfu brothers this spring was discovered, and the disturbed soil was taken out, which was the original pit dug by the Chen family to find Zhou Dynasty bronzes. To the west of the pit, at a distance of four inches from the ground, traces of a coffin and half a human skeleton were found. The skull and upper limbs were missing, and only the leg bones remained. Fragments of the skull were found in the disturbed soil, which was probably destroyed by the Chen brothers when they were digging for antiquities. It can now be determined that this is a tomb, and the steel artifacts unearthed in the spring were burial objects. The steel artifacts were in a pit about eight or nine inches from the ground, with a section of matting next to it, with decayed wood blocks and debris on it. The burial bronzes were arranged in order here. There is also a large tree, with branches at the top, about four meters long, lying horizontally in the soil from west to east, probably used to cover the coffin and burial objects. The original form and scope of the tomb are currently under discussion. Director Wang (Xiantang) previously suspected that the Zhou Dynasty bronzes unearthed from this place were stored in wooden boxes. Now this problem has been completely solved. They are burial objects, not storage objects. The following two points can prove this: First, any storage of ancient objects must be in a place where people once lived, and the architecture is commensurate with the artifacts. When the pit was first opened, large and small round pits were discovered, but there was no large-scale architecture on the ground, which we found very strange. Now we know that these fourteen heavy artifacts (the tripods, plates, Yi, etc. from the spring) are objects from the tomb and have nothing to do with the site. (2) When the bronzes were first discovered, there were still complete fish bones in the tripod. It is said that there was also a bone in another tripod, similar to a lamb leg bone. There is no reason to store food and utensils together. Therefore, based on our excavation and research, it can be determined that the Zhou Dynasty bronzes discovered in the spring were indeed burial objects and not storage objects. Our initial purpose in excavating this place was to find clues to the relics of the Small Zhu State from the bronzes discovered in the spring and to compare them with the relics of the ancient states of Teng and Xue. According to our current investigation, this place (Gutuiding) was already in ruins before the Spring and Autumn and Warring States periods, so the people of the Small Zhu State sought this higher mound as a burial place for their ancestors, and it is not the site of the Small Zhu State. According to the burial situation here, it is quite similar to the tombs in Xincun, Junxian, Henan, which was the atmosphere of the Spring and Autumn and Warring States periods. Such things as wooden frames, mats, and red paint were all customs at the time. It is determined to be the tomb of a noble of the Small Zhu State. The relationship of this person to the burial bronzes may be found in the inscriptions on the bronzes. Later, the tomb was turned into farmland and gradually leveled, and then discovered by the Chen Shangfu brothers. Our future work here will continue to excavate in order to find the contents of the site, such as large and small round pits and all the artifacts, pottery shards, bones, stones, etc. Even a small thing can be investigated for its origin. In our eyes, its value is no different from precious bronzes, and it can arouse our great research interest. At the moment, we are starting to wash the pottery shards, bones, and other miscellaneous items that have already been excavated, immediately numbering and registering them one by one and noting the location of the pit from which they were unearthed and the depth from the ground, and then comparing and studying them separately. As for the Anshang site, in addition to excavation work, I also tried to investigate and collect ancient steles and inscriptions and investigate the establishment dates of villages near this site as evidence. For example, at the western end of this village, there is a Laojun Hall (temple, now more than half collapsed). In the late Song Dynasty, a Taoist named Chao Ranzhi built a house here and called it Xiuzhen Temple. During the Zhengzong period of the Yuan Dynasty, his disciples began to rebuild it as Laojun Hall. The oldest inscription on the stele was erected in the tenth year of the Ming Dynasty, and the names of the villages that donated money to build this hall are engraved on it. There is no Anshangyi among them. In the early Kangxi period of the Qing Dynasty, there was only the name Anshangyi. An'an and Jun are the same. Later, An was called An. I further investigated the Chen family's tombstones and learned that their distant ancestor, Chen Yingke, came here at the end of the Ming Dynasty, and there are now fifteen generations. This village has no other surnames. The Chen family can be regarded as a representative of the patriarchal society of our country. Knowing that the Chen family came in the late Ming Dynasty, it can be inferred that the opening up of the nearby mountainous area, the leveling of Gutuiding (Anshang site), and the appearance of the bronze tomb were all the work of the Chen family. This is also extremely relevant and interesting material in this excavation of antiquities.

At the same time as Gutuiding, the Caowang Tomb was also being excavated. Work began on the 26th, because the tomb had been uncovered by local people with three stone pits. Mou Xiangnong, Pan Ke, and Liu Xuepeng each guarded one pit, hiring fifteen workers in total. The daily wage was also 30 cents of silver. Mou guarded the first pit, Liu guarded the second pit, and Pan guarded the third pit. Each led five workers. The first two pits are on the top of the mountain and are relatively close. The third pit is slightly farther away and is at the northern end, and the terrain is also relatively low. The yellow soil and stones in each pit had been almost completely removed by the 30th. The structural forms of the three pits are different. Generally, the front part is a stone chamber, and there is a square hole in the ceiling above the chamber. It is a kind of black stone building. Viewers can descend from the ceiling along the ladder. The height can meet the top. The rear part is the tomb, which is two holes. In the middle, there may be flat stone pillars or large round stones lying down. There are no inscriptions. The depth of the front chamber of the first pit is 1.9 meters. There is a small stone chamber on the left and right of the car, probably for placing the burial objects. The horizontal stone above the tomb has a fish-shaped pattern carved on it, which is very rough. The depth of the front chamber of the second pit is 1.8 meters, and there is only one small stone chamber on the west side. The pattern of the square victory shape is also not exquisite. The third pit is slightly larger than the previous two pits, with a depth of 2.2 meters. There are two small stone chambers on the east side, which communicate with each other, separated by prismatic small stone pillars. The stone pillars of the entire pit are the same. According to Pan Ke, this kind of prismatic stone pillar has a Western style, and the pattern is also fish-shaped. The tomb door on the west side has been broken. According to Mou Xiangnong, the daily work situation and the estimation of the discovered items are briefly stated that since we started work on the 26th, we have not seen anything except rubble and yellow soil excavated from each pit. On the 27th, the work of lifting stones and taking soil continued. In the morning, five stones were dug out of the yellow soil and rubble. One of them was carved very finely. In the afternoon, a broken piece of a "pot" was dug out under the stone pillar in the pit. On the morning of the 28th, the bottom of the tomb was already visible, all of which were stone bottoms. Many pottery shards, a lead hairpin, a broken sword, and the mouth of a broken bottle were dug out in the front chamber of the tomb. More than one broken five-zhu coin and a piece of the roof of a burial object were discovered. On the 29th, it was Sunday, and we rested as usual for one day. As of today (30th), a total of fourteen five-zhu coins, a broken sword, a lead hairpin, two roofs of burial objects that can be connected completely, which are also pottery, and many other broken pottery shards and bones have been obtained. According to our speculation, it can be determined that this place must have been the tomb of a noble at that time. There must have been other great buildings above the ground, such as sacrificial halls and sacrificial pavilions. Now the stone foundation is still there next to the first pit, and there are many Jing Tong around the cemetery nearby, or they were buildings at that time, which were destroyed and moved later. According to the pottery manufacturing, carving patterns, five-zhu coins, lead hairpins and other items, it can be determined that its era was indeed the Eastern Han Dynasty. As for the bones excavated, they cannot be used as a basis, because these three pits have been excavated by people, and it is unknown how many times they have been through. The original bones have long been lost. In the future, if we continue to excavate the tombs next to it, or get epitaphs or carved characters on the stones, and then combine them with the overall research, we can fully understand and know it. Now, if we only speculate based on one corner and one thing, I am afraid that there will be some differences from what is expected in the future. Today, only the stone soil in the second pit has not been completely extracted and cleaned, which is considered a stage. At the moment, we are planning to open other tombs and pits. We will discuss with Committee Member Dong about where to start first, and then we can start excavation. (October 30)

Qingdao Agricultural Products Exhibition - 30,000 Farmers Participate - Shen Honglie Attends and Delivers a Speech 95

Qingdao Correspondence. In order to promote the improvement of rural agricultural products, the Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs, together with the Agricultural and Forestry Office, held an agricultural products exhibition to compare and improve and appointed Zhou Yaqing, the head of the agricultural affairs section of the Agricultural and Forestry Office, and Yuan Lixiu, the director of the agricultural and commercial stock of the Social Bureau, as the chief and deputy directors of the preparation committee. In advance, they ordered the construction offices of each township to earnestly collect products and send them to the exhibition for display. They also sent letters to various places along the Jiaoji Railway to solicit special products for reference. This exhibition of agricultural products has received more than eighty kinds, more than two thousand items, which were held at 10:00 am on October 30. The exhibition will last for three days. The venue is set up in the Licun Farm. In the middle is a lecture stage, and on both sides are the agricultural product exhibition areas, which are divided into five departments: (1) Agronomy Department, (2) Horticulture Department, (3) Animal Husbandry Department, (4) Forestry Department, (5) Pest and Disease Department. All kinds of agricultural crops and specimens are collected in each department. About 30,000 farmers participated. After the opening ceremony, Ge Jingying, the director of the Rural Office, chaired the meeting and reported the significance of the opening ceremony, briefly stating the purpose of this agricultural products exhibition: (1) To improve agriculture by scientific methods; (2) To collect various agricultural products, compare and observe, and use them as specimens for improvement; (3) To enable farmers to have a clear understanding of new agriculture and use it as a reference. After the report, Mayor Shen Honglie delivered a speech, briefly stating that today's agricultural products exhibition is the second time that Qingdao has held such an exhibition in six or seven years. More than two thousand agricultural products have been received, which shows that farmers are very interested in this. I have a rare opportunity to say a few words to you. First, it is necessary to study agriculture in the Jiaozhou area, because the soil of each township in this city is mostly barren and the area is extremely small. Even in Licun District alone, there are only more than 37,000 mu of cultivated land, but the population is more than 70,000. According to the average calculation, each person only gets half a mu of land. Agricultural products are already lacking and insufficient to maintain life. In the future, the population will increase day by day, and the land allocated to each person will also decrease day by day. Farmers' lives will be impossible to maintain. Therefore, in order to relieve farmers' suffering, it is necessary to improve agricultural products and increase production efficiency. Second, methods to improve agriculture: A. Select seeds. If fruit seedlings, vegetable seedlings, etc., are not selected good varieties, the harvest will not be abundant. The Agricultural and Forestry Office has very good honey peaches. The price of peaches is four or five times higher than other varieties. It is possible to imitate planting. Also, Licun is suitable for pears, and the Zhan Mountain area is suitable for grapes, so the selection of seeds should also vary according to the terrain. B. Eliminate pests. If pests occur in fruit trees, the harvest will be reduced and must be removed. For example, last year, the pear trees had cow and sheep hair mites, so the pears did not mature. This year, the township construction office provided medicine to spray pesticides for prevention. As a result, the pears were full of fruit, and the harvest was doubled compared to previous years. It is estimated that the total income from pears alone this year is about 600,000 yuan. At the moment, the Agricultural and Forestry Office has set up a pest and disease department to specifically prepare to eliminate pests for various agricultural products and strive to increase production. Third, methods of planting land. Agricultural improvement is not only a matter of excellent seeds that can be perfectly solved. Operating technology also has a great relationship, but our country's farmers are stubborn and old-fashioned and unwilling to apply new methods. At the moment, the Agricultural and Forestry Office has established a promotion and experimental area in various townships to rent farmers' land for experiments. Farmers have a considerable understanding of all the achievements, and we will continue to add to them in the future to make it easier for farmers to observe, so the new method can be promoted without hindrance. In addition, I would like to mention two things: 1. I hope that farmers in various departments will plant more fruit trees, because the income from one mu of fruit trees can be worth 20 mu of good land. In the future, if fruit trees are promoted, the income of this city will naturally increase. 2. I hope to plant more vegetables. The Agricultural and Forestry Office has good seeds of vegetables that Westerners like. If we can imitate planting and supply them to foreigners, the annual income will also be considerable.

The exhibition will be held for three days. There will be agricultural lectures and costume lectures every day to impart agricultural knowledge and distribute publications so that farmers can spread the information and gradually change their self-enclosed mentality. As for the farmers who come to the exhibition to visit, the guidance personnel of the association will explain in detail, so the farmers are all happy. (October 31)

Hunan Provincial Government Establishes a Western Hunan Rehabilitation Office - Destroying the Power of the Western Hunan Indigenous Chieftains - Reorganizing Western Hunan Military and Political Affairs 97

Changsha Correspondence. The seven counties of Zhijiang, Qianyang, Huangxian, Huitong, Jingxian, Suining, and Tongdao in western Hunan, adjacent to Guizhou and Guangxi, are far from the provincial capital and have always been occupied by indigenous chieftains. Although they are nominally under the jurisdiction of the Hunan Provincial Government, they are actually within the sphere of influence of the heroes of the Hunan-Guizhou green forests. In the past, Chen Hanzhang, Chen Wo, He Jingcheng, Yao Jiyu, and others were all based in these seven counties to develop their power. The provincial government could not reach them, and the transportation was inconvenient, so there was nothing to be done. He Jian recently sent Li Jue's department of the 19th Division to defeat Chen Wo and recover Zhijiang, and established the Fourth Security District Command in Hongjiang, with Li Jue as the commander, and these seven counties as the area of jurisdiction. Four regiments of provincial troops were dispatched to be stationed regularly, intending to fundamentally destroy the power of the indigenous chieftains. A rehabilitation office was established in the district command to promote politics with military power. Yesterday, the provincial government committee meeting on the 27th decided to entrust Li Jue with the task of handling the rehabilitation affairs of the seven counties in western Hunan and appointed Peng Zhuo as the director of the rehabilitation office, who will handle the rehabilitation of civil, financial, educational, and construction affairs in the seven counties in accordance with Li Jue's orders. The measures for the rehabilitation of officials in the counties of western Hunan prescribed by the provincial government are recorded as follows: (1) The commander of the 4th Security District shall temporarily handle the rehabilitation affairs of the seven counties of Zhijiang, Qianyang, Huangxian, Jingxian, Huitong, Suining, and Tongdao under his jurisdiction in accordance with the orders of the Hunan Provincial Government. (2) The rehabilitation matters of civil affairs, finance, education, and construction in the counties listed in the preceding article shall be handled by the county governments under the supervision of the district commander, but major matters shall still be submitted to the Hunan Provincial Government for approval. (3) For the convenience of handling rehabilitation, the district commander shall set up a rehabilitation office in the district command, and the district commander shall issue documents to the outside world in his name. (4) The rehabilitation office shall have one director, who shall manage the affairs of the office and direct and supervise the staff under his command in accordance with the orders of the district commander and the guidance of the chief of staff. (5) The rehabilitation office shall have five staff members. (6) The director and staff members shall be appointed or commissioned by the Hunan Provincial Government upon the recommendation of the district commander. (7) The rehabilitation office may establish a number of clerks and secretaries in accordance with the complexity of the affairs. (8) The detailed rules for the rehabilitation office shall be formulated separately. (9) The rehabilitation office shall be abolished when the rehabilitation affairs of each county are completed. (10) If there are any unfulfilled matters in these measures, the district commander may submit them to the Hunan Provincial Government for revision. (11) These measures shall be implemented from the date of approval by the Hunan Provincial Government. (October 28)

Anhui Provincial Department of Civil Affairs Prepares to Establish a Bureau for Opium Suppression 丨 Following the Example of Hubei Province and Considering Implementation丨 98

Anqing correspondence: The Anhui Provincial Government recently received an order from the General Headquarters for Bandit Suppression in Henan, Hubei, and Anhui Provinces to implement a six-year opium prohibition plan. It also issued regulations to subordinate areas for registering opium addicts and strictly prohibiting them from smoking; strictly banning the sale of narcotic drugs and closing opium dens; and strictly prohibiting the planting of opium in inland provinces and banning the purchase of opium produced in border areas. Among these regulations, those concerning the issuance and renewal of licenses and the collection of license fees, as well as restrictions on opium dens, stipulate that the provincial government should designate a competent authority to handle these matters. The Anhui Provincial Government has decided that the Department of Civil Affairs will be the competent authority and will establish a bureau within the department to specifically handle opium suppression affairs throughout the province. The Department of Civil Affairs has also drafted organizational regulations for the opium suppression office and a provisional budget. The proposed organization of the office is based on the model of the Hubei Provincial Department of Civil Affairs, with some adjustments. The budget is approximately two-fifths less than that of the Hubei Provincial Department of Civil Affairs' opium suppression office. It has already been approved by the provincial government meeting on October 27th, and the establishment is expected to occur soon. (October 31st)

Jiangsu Provincial Government Establishes a County Magistrate Qualification Review Committee Qualified Personnel will be Recorded by the Department of Civil Affairs for Future Use 99

Chairman of the Jiangsu Provincial Government, Chen Guofu, and Director of the Department of Civil Affairs, Gu Renfa, have established a County Magistrate Qualification Review Committee to select county magistrates and improve local governance. The regulations for this committee have been approved by the provincial government's 605th meeting. The original text is as follows:

Article 1: These regulations are based on the provincial government's 603rd meeting. Article 2: All members of the provincial government will serve as members of this committee. Article 3: When the committee meets, the chairman of the provincial government will serve as the chairman. If the chairman is unable to attend due to circumstances, the Director of the Department of Civil Affairs will serve as the acting chairman. Article 4: The standards for the committee's review of county magistrates will be based on Article 1 of the revised Regulations for the Appointment of County Magistrates promulgated by the National Government, as well as Article 3 of the Regulations for the Appointment of Civil Servants, and Article 2 of the Provisional Measures for Restricting the Appointment of County Magistrates promulgated by the General Headquarters for Bandit Suppression in Henan, Anhui, and Hubei Provinces. Article 5: The following three categories of personnel (1), (2), and (3) may request review from this committee. Personnel in category (4) must be introduced and submitted to the committee for review by two or more members of the provincial government who will take responsibility. (1) Those who have passed the central higher examinations and been assigned to this province. (2) Those who have passed the first and second county magistrate examinations in this province. (3) Those who have been previously selected and qualified by this province. (4) Those recommended from various sources. Article 6: After reviewing the qualifications of those under review and confirming that they meet the requirements of these regulations, the committee members will conduct separate inquiries and investigate their past conduct and abilities. Those deemed suitable for the position of county magistrate by the committee will be recorded by the Department of Civil Affairs for future use. Article 7: If any of the following circumstances apply to a person under review, their record will be revoked, even if they have passed the review: (1) Those who have engaged in counter-revolutionary activities. (2) Those who have been expelled from the party or have had their party rights suspended. (3) Those who have engaged in corrupt or unethical behavior. (4) Those who have been removed from office after a thorough investigation and found guilty with evidence. (5) Those who have been sentenced to imprisonment. (6) Those who have been declared bankrupt. (7) Those who smoke opium. Article 8: If it is discovered that a person under review has falsified their qualifications, they will not only be denied review or have their record revoked, but will also be handed over to the court for legal action. Article 9: The committee may request personnel from the provincial government's secretariat and the Department of Civil Affairs as needed. Article 10: Detailed rules for the committee's operations will be determined separately. Article 11: If there are any omissions in these regulations, they may be revised by the provincial government committee at any time. Article 12: These regulations will be implemented upon approval by the provincial government committee. (November 2nd)

The Issue of Establishing a Local Court 100

A local court was established in this county during the early years of the Republic of China. However, judicial affairs were abolished when Yuan Shikai declared himself emperor and were handled by the county government. It was not until the previous year that a county court was established. The Jiangsu Higher Court and other courts previously planned to establish local courts in all counties, and this county was included in the plan. Yesterday, Lin Biao, the president of the Higher Court, visited Songjiang to inspect the prison and detention center. He discussed the establishment of a local court with County Magistrate Jin, Court President Wang Sixian, and Chief Prosecutor Zhu, which would have jurisdiction over the five counties of Songjiang, Fengxian, Jinshan, Qingpu, and Nanhui, as well as the original plan to build a prison. The construction drawings and material cost estimates had been submitted to the Higher Court for review and approval by the Judicial Administration Department. In addition to allocating funds from the surtax on legal documents, the construction costs were still significantly insufficient and would require local fundraising. The fundraising methods have not yet been decided and will be discussed with County Magistrate Jin and submitted to the Prison Improvement Association for deliberation and implementation. Finally, he inquired in detail about the Songjiang Bank bankruptcy case and the work of the liquidation office. He returned to Shanghai by night train and is reportedly scheduled to inspect other counties.

Murder Case Occurs Outside Panmen 102

Ni Yugan, a 22-year-old man from Yangzhou, came to Suzhou five years ago to work as an apprentice at the Runchang Foreign Machinery Store at No. 5 Yejia Lane outside Changmen. He had already completed his apprenticeship and earned an annual salary of 100 yuan. He was hardworking and thrifty and highly valued by his employer. On the 20th day of the previous lunar month, he returned to his hometown due to his mother's illness. He returned to Suzhou on the 27th and went to the store on the 30th. Nanhui

The Sea Wall in the County is in Critical Condition, Requiring Substantial Funds for Repair 103

The Nanhui County area suffered two typhoons last month, damaging over 40 li of the coastal sea wall. Thanks to strenuous emergency repairs at the time, a complete collapse was averted. Plans are now underway for repairs, but the project requires more than 140,000 yuan. County Magistrate Yuan Xiluo is seeking funds locally and requesting appropriations from the province. The details are as follows: The county suffered the most severe typhoon damage in recent years. The disaster-stricken people lacked food and clothing and were in dire need of assistance. The Sichuan-Southern Chongbaoqi Five County Flood Relief Association, the Pudong Association of Compatriots, and various charitable organizations such as Huayang Yizhen raised and distributed relief rice, clothing, and seeds. The local government and gentry also raised funds to provide economic relief. County Magistrate Yuan Xiluo, considering the severe damage to the county's sea wall, urgently needed repairs and convened local gentry for discussions. It was decided to implement a work-relief program. The most critical Litang section would be repaired this year, and the Wanggongtang Port would be dredged to clear water sources. In addition to raising funds locally, a request for subsidies would be submitted to the provincial government, as the two major projects of repairing Litang and dredging Wanggongtang Port required a substantial 140,000 yuan, which could not be fully raised locally. On the 30th of last month, County Magistrate Yuan Xiluo, accompanied by Construction Director Ling Zhibin, went to Zhenjiang to meet with Provincial Chairman Chen Guofu, Director of the Department of Civil Affairs Gu Renfa, Director of the Department of Finance Zhao Dihua, and Director of the Department of Construction Shen Baixian to personally report on the critical situation of the Nanhui sea wall and request provincial funds for repairs to implement the work-relief program this winter. Yuan and Ling returned to Shanghai yesterday. It is reported that the provincial government will submit the matter for discussion at a meeting.

Wuxi

A Solution Has Been Found for the Debts of the Huisheng Factory 104

The absconding of Xi Huian, the owner of Huisheng Silk Factory, due to debts, has caused complications, including disturbances by female workers and the smashing of counters at the Chamber of Commerce, as reported in this newspaper. It is now learned that the County Chamber of Commerce has provisionally formulated three solutions based on various opinions and investigations into the factory's situation: (1) The Silk Factory Association should supervise the factory personnel left behind to verify the worker accounts and, according to Xi Huian's letter, first sell the eight bales of silk in storage and the by-products and raw materials in the factory to pay wages. If this is insufficient, the 417 bales of dried cocoons of Ruichangrun, Xinchunqian should be sold, as the warehouse receipts were used to secure loans from firms. These loans should be deducted first, and the remaining funds should be used to supplement wage payments, and the workers should be dismissed. The Silk Factory Association will be responsible for these matters. (2) It has been found that, in addition to the Ruichangrun, Xinchunqian cocoons used for wages, the factory has 141 bales of Ruichangrun summer and autumn cocoons, 2,080 bales of Yixin autumn cocoons, and 318 bales of Xiesheng autumn cocoons, totaling 2,539 bales of dried cocoons. All warehouse receipts have been used to secure loans from various banks and money shops, totaling 19,915.19 yuan from Jiaotong Bank, 8,013.54 yuan from Xingye Bank, and 16,226.44 yuan from Duanchangrun Bank, plus 14,000 yuan from Changzhou Taicheng Bank and 6,100 yuan from Yutong Bank, for a total of 64,255.17 yuan. Now that the factory has ceased operations, the banks and money shops should consider the market conditions and sell the cocoons to settle the loans. Any remaining funds should be held in trust by the banks and money shops and distributed equally among the creditors in the future. However, the amount of dried cocoons used by the machines should be reported to the Chamber of Commerce and the silk factory and cocoon industry associations at any time, and personnel should be sent to check the quantity and weight. (3) According to the list sent by Xi Huian and the subsequent report from Chicheng Coal Company, the factory owes another 4,114.50 yuan for coal and other debts. If there are any remaining funds, they should be distributed equally. The zero-lot cocoon holders should be informed to return to their hometowns for the time being and not wait in the city. The Chamber of Commerce can only handle the matter on a fair basis. If creditors have other claims, they can submit them to the authorities for verification. The above measures were sent by the Chamber of Commerce to the parties concerned yesterday for joint implementation. At the same time, in view of the previous disturbances by female workers, the Chamber of Commerce has specifically requested the county government to pay attention and suppress any disturbances at any time. Zhou Wei, the representative of the factory staff, sold the silk in the factory according to Xi Huian's letter and obtained 4,851.668 yuan to pay the first installment of wages. When this was learned by creditors such as Li Xiaocheng, they argued with Zhou, leading to a fight and mutual wrestling that were brought to the first sub-bureau of the Public Security Bureau for settlement. It is also reported that more than a dozen workers from Xi Huian's hometown (Zhoutang Town, Jiangyin) have occupied his home to demand debts, which has not yet been resolved.

Rice and Bean Merchants Switch to New Measures 105

The county government has repeatedly instructed various trade associations to switch to the new system of weights and measures as soon as possible. Industries such as silk and cloth have complied with the order, but the rice, bean, and miscellaneous grain industries have delayed implementation due to the new measures not yet being manufactured. Recently, the county government ordered the two industries to switch to the new system for all scales and measures from November 1st, and no violations would be tolerated. The two industries, after receiving the order, felt that the new system was smaller than the old system, about 94 percent of the old standard. If implemented, the related expenses of warehouse rent, water transportation, measuring, and labor costs would inevitably be reduced accordingly. They have submitted the difficulties to the county government, requesting consideration and overall planning, and calling relevant parties to determine a balanced solution. At present, the new measures have been manufactured, and implementation can begin as soon as the county government agrees on a solution.

Jiaxing

Petition to Waive the Closing of the Sub-Customs 109

The Jiaxing Hangzhou Customs sub-office has been established for decades. The Ministry of Finance has now ordered the Hangzhou Customs to close the Jiaxing sub-office. Local businesses were alarmed upon hearing this. If the Jiaxing sub-office is closed, the local products exported from Jiaxing and its surrounding areas will have to be reported to the Hangzhou Customs, which will have a significant impact on both time and expense. To maintain the convenience of exporting local products, the County Chamber of Commerce has resolved at its 14th executive committee meeting to telegraph the Ministry of Finance to revoke the decision and exempt the Jiaxing sub-office from closure.

Jiashan

A Bandit's Body was Found Floating in the Dang 110

A nameless corpse with numerous wounds was found in Xiangfu Dang in the county area the other day (the 31st). The local police retrieved the body and reported it to the authorities for inspection. Someone later identified the corpse as Xiao Bajin, a notorious bandit from Pudong. He was usually extremely fierce and had committed numerous crimes in the vicinity of Zhouzhuang and in Wu County. He was reportedly killed by his accomplices due to a dispute over stolen goods, and his body was dumped into the Dang.

Pinghu

Attempted Rape and Eight Savage Slashes 111

There is a nun named Miaoxiang, about 27 or 28 years old, from Haiyan, residing in the Guanyin Temple in Xindai Town. Last night, Quan Rong, a local hooligan, climbed over the wall with a bamboo pole and broke into her bedroom, intending to rape her. Miaoxiang resisted desperately and shouted loudly. Quan Rong then used a pre-prepared knife to slash her eight times, hoping to kill her and silence her. Neighbors heard the alarm and rushed to the scene. Miaoxiang was lying in a pool of blood but was still able to speak. She was rushed to the hospital for treatment. The assailant, Quan Rong, fled without a trace.

A group of bandits, armed with guns, suddenly arrived in Chen Daqiao in the fifth district of the county the other day and robbed every household. In the case of a farmer named Liu, the bandits could not find much money in his house. They forced him to reveal where the hidden money was, but he refused. The bandits then burned down all his houses. The losses are said to be enormous.

According to Xin Sheng News Agency, after the resignation of Finance Minister Song Ziwen, the new Finance Minister Kong Xiangxi has formally taken office. According to inquiries with banking circles yesterday, neither the financial nor financial markets were affected in the slightest during the transition between the two finance ministers, so everything remains the same. There are no changes. The 20 million yuan treasury bills from the Song Ziwen era have already been allocated for bandit suppression military expenses. It is expected that the Ministry of Finance and the banking community will not have any new contacts in the near future, as the strength of the national banks and commercial banks can no longer bear any more burdens. However, it is difficult to predict at this time whether the new Finance Minister Kong Xiangxi will have any policies to discuss with the banking community in the future.

Xin Sheng News Agency reported that there are more than 200 French expatriates residing in Shanghai who have been awarded medals by the French government. Considering it to be a social honor, they will gather all the individuals holding French medals at the French Consulate General in Shanghai tomorrow to organize the French Medal Association in China. The meeting will be held immediately and presided over by Consul General Mery to discuss the significance of the association and to strengthen diplomatic ties between France and China. Former Chinese Finance Minister Song Ziwen was elected honorary president, as the French President awarded him a special honorary medal during his visit to France. Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Implements Joint Transportation for Shaoxing-Shanghai Passengers Contract Signed with Xiaoshao Long-Distance Bus Company, Effective Yesterday 116

The Traffic Department of the Two-Line Administration and the Xiaoshao Long-Distance Bus Company, in order to facilitate the convenience of passengers between Shaoxing and Shanghai, signed a joint passenger transportation contract, which is roughly as follows: (1) Joint transportation stations, on the railway side, are Kongchen Bridge, Chang'an, Xieqiao, Xiashi, Jiaxing, Jiashan, Songjiang, Shangnan, Shangbei, and Jiuzhan. On the bus side, they are Wuyun, Chang'an, Beihai, Shaoxing, Keqiao, Ruanshe, Yaqian, Xiaoshan, and Jiudian. Both parties may sell joint tickets to each other. The validity period of the tickets is stipulated as within two days from the date of sale. (2) Joint passenger tickets are of the joint-ticket type. Fares are determined based on the fare that each party should receive. At the end of each month, both parties should mutually submit a table with the number of tickets received, serial numbers, dates, and levels for verification. (3) For joint transportation of luggage and packages, those shipped from the railway joint transportation station will be delivered to the bus company by porters dispatched by the Railway Bureau after arriving at Nanxing Bridge, and the bus company will sign for them. Those shipped from the bus joint transportation station will be delivered to the Railway Bureau by porters dispatched by the company after arriving at Sanlang Temple, and the Railway Bureau will sign for them. The company is responsible for handling the procedures for crossing the river. (4) Settlement of accounts. The joint transportation fares will be settled once a month and paid by both parties before the 10th of each month. (5) Term. The effective term of the contract is tentatively set for one year. If neither party proposes any modifications three months before the expiration date, it can be extended for another year in sequence. The contract was implemented on November 1st.

Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Writes to Domestic Manufacturers to Reduce Prices of Domestic Goods 117

Foreign Goods are Eliminating Themselves without Boycott The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce wrote to domestic manufacturers yesterday, stating: "We received a letter from the Jiangsu Provincial Chamber of Commerce Federation on the 1st of this month, stating that at the second meeting of our membership congress, a proposal from the Sisui Town Chamber of Commerce stated, 'Foreigners price their goods very cheaply at the beginning, without considering costs or profits. Later, after their businesses develop, they gradually increase prices to seize huge profits. Chinese merchants do the opposite. Once goods are sold, they calculate all costs and profits, regardless of whether they sell well or not, and set an extremely high price. This is why foreign goods flood the market and domestic goods sell poorly. To revitalize industry, it is necessary to persuade all manufacturers to reduce the value of domestic goods. If we cannot recover our rights and interests, we will be ruined.' The proposal was immediately submitted to the congress for discussion. Everyone agreed that although domestic goods have shown rapid progress in recent years, foreign goods still flood the market because foreign goods have low costs and low prices, while domestic goods have high costs and high prices. This has led to the trend of foreign goods being dumped. If all major manufacturers can reduce prices, consumers will be happy to buy domestic goods given the weak economic situation of the people. In this way, foreign goods will eliminate themselves without a boycott." It was resolved to record the case and send a letter to your association to handle it. We hereby record the case and inform you, hoping you will handle it accordingly. It is indeed a good way to reduce the selling price of goods so that customers are happy to buy them and easily promote sales, thereby resisting the dumping of foreign goods. Following the previous letters, we have written subsequent letters to notify you, hoping you will investigate and handle it, and also widely persuade and adopt this principle to all domestic manufacturers under your jurisdiction. We earnestly expect this.

Both Exports and Imports Sharply Decline in the First Half of This Year The Trade Deficit is Even Worse Than Last Year 118

According to the Central News Agency, in recent years, the export aspect of China's foreign trade has gradually decreased, while the import aspect has increased year by year. Last year, exports decreased to 492,641,000 customs taels, imports increased to 1,049,147,000 customs taels, and the trade deficit was 556,605,000 customs taels, which is a historical high. As for the situation of China's foreign trade in the first half of this year, both exports and imports have generally declined, with imports declining even more. The Central News Agency reporter specially inquired with He Bingxian, Director of the International Trade Bureau, at the bureau yesterday. He explained in detail the reasons for the decline, and his remarks are recorded as follows.

Production Declines, Exports Sharply Decline 119

In recent years, domestic disasters have been frequent, so the productivity has gradually decreased year by year. Exported goods have also declined sharply, and this year is even more severe. From January to June of this year, the total number of exports was 474,641,566 yuan. January was 39,619,728 yuan, 39.09 percent compared to the same month last year. February was 63,165,622 yuan, 55.68 percent compared to the same month last year. March was 101,747,410 yuan, 69.19 percent compared to the same month last year. April was 109,987,508 yuan, 74.72 percent compared to the same month last year. May was 100,225,792 yuan, 66.05 percent compared to the same month last year. June was 59,895,496 yuan, 54.4 percent compared to the same month last year.

After the Implementation of Railway Responsible Joint Transport, the First Shanghai-Beiping Freight Car Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday The Regulations Stipulate One Round Trip Per Day Between Shanghai and Beiping If Goods are Crowded, Special Shanghai-Beiping Freight Cars Can Be Opened 120

After the implementation of responsible freight joint transport by national railways the other day, the Jinpu Railway Bureau requested that armed soldiers be stationed at the Nanjing Pukou riverside to protect the through Shanghai-Beiping freight train. After the resumption of traffic, the 402nd Shanghai-Beiping freight train that departed from Shanghai Maigen Road Station at 5:20 PM the other day arrived at Nanjing Riverside at 6:40 AM yesterday, crossed the river by ferry, and is scheduled to arrive at Beiping Qianmen Station at 12:12 PM tomorrow. The 401st Shanghai-Beiping freight train that departed from Beiping Qianmen Station on October 28th was prevented from passing through the Pukou riverside on the 30th by Pukou stevedores. After troops were dispatched to protect it, it boarded the ferry the other day and crossed south of the Yangtze River. It arrived at Shanghai Maigen Road Station at 8:51 AM yesterday. The train was fully loaded with goods from Shanghai and Zhabei. As for the 401st Shanghai-Beiping freight train that departed from Beiping the other day, it is scheduled to arrive in Shanghai at 6:40 AM tomorrow. The 402nd Shanghai-Beiping freight train departing from Shanghai Maigen Road Station at 5:20 PM yesterday will arrive in Beiping in five days. It is stipulated that there will be one round trip per day between Shanghai and Beiping, but if goods are crowded, special Shanghai-Beiping freight trains can be opened.

○ ○ ○ ○

Foreign Goods Imports Decline Even More 121

In the first half of this year, the sharp decline in China's exports has been mentioned above. At the same time, the number of foreign goods imported has also declined sharply. As a percentage, the decline in foreign goods imports is even greater than the decline in domestic goods exports. However, comparing the number of exports and imports in the first half of this year, the trade deficit is more than 5,517,000 yuan. The trade deficit for the same period last year was 30,818,900 customs taels, which is equivalent to 48,015,846.7 yuan. The biggest reason for the sharp decline in foreign goods imports is due to the decline in the purchasing power of the Chinese people. The increase in import tariffs is also a reason.

Relief Measures Encourage Production 122

When the reporter continued to inquire about what measures could be taken to relieve the sharp decline in exports, the response was that relieving the sharp decline in exports is a very big problem that cannot be described in a few words. The domestic rural economy has gradually declined, resulting in a decrease in productivity, which has affected exports. Therefore, the fundamental relief measure is to adjust rural finance and encourage production, but this cannot be successful in a year or two. He then discussed the establishment of a special bureau for trade with Russia by the Ministry of Industry, but there are still no new developments.

Furthermore, a company of Yu Zhishan's troops is currently stationed in southern (6) The current Japanese governance policy in Manchukuo is to alienate the Volunteer Army from the people."

After Eight Rice Dealers Cancelled Contracts for Private Purchase of Japanese Rice, the Association Resolved to Temporarily End the Matter 125

The Guomin News Agency reports that the case of eight rice dealers, including Yongda, purchasing Japanese rice in this city has been subjected to public condemnation. Although they have already announced the cancellation of the contracts and compensated the American merchant Handao Lai Foreign Firm for a loss of 10,000 yuan, all sectors believe that they are to blame and advocate for further punishment to serve as a warning. The city's Grain Food Committee recently held a meeting and resolved to instruct the Miscellaneous Grain Industry Association to convene its own meeting to decide on a punishment method. The resulting fines will be allocated to the warehouse fund. It is now learned that the Miscellaneous Grain Association has already replied yesterday, stating that they were indeed unaware of the Japanese rice purchased by the eight rice dealers beforehand. They only knew that it was Saigon small-grained rice handled by the American merchant Handao Lai, and they purchased it because it was cheap. However, after the Japanese rice was discovered and warned by the Association, they immediately complied with the order to cancel the contracts and compensate for the losses, which amounted to 10,000 yuan. The Association has now notified its members that they must not knowingly violate the rules and purchase it privately for profit. Otherwise, once discovered, they will immediately be expelled from the Association and announced to all sectors, and everyone will abandon them. As for further punishment, given the current commercial decline and economic panic, which have reached an extreme point, it seems that it is indeed difficult to bear. Therefore, it has been resolved to temporarily end the matter.

Shanghai Farmers Oppose Shanghai Middle School's Land Grab; Petition Municipal Council Members 126

The Provincial Shanghai Middle School recently purchased over four *mu* of farmland in the Wujiaxiang area of Caoding District in western Shanghai, along the Shanghai-Minhang long-distance bus route, as the school's new site. It submitted a request to the Ministry of Interior, which was forwarded to the Shanghai Municipal Land Bureau to be handled in accordance with Article 4 of the Land Acquisition Law. Upon learning of this, the farmers were panic-stricken. They jointly petitioned the Municipal Government, the Bureau of Education, and the Ministry of Interior, requesting the revocation of the order and the finding of another location to protect the farmers' livelihoods. To date, no instructions have been received. Unexpectedly, the farmers received a notification from the Land Bureau the day before yesterday and were extremely angry. They went to the head of the district, Zhu Jinyu, and the local warden, Jin Ziwei, to make a scene. Zhu and Jin were unable to persuade them and had to lead the masses to the Caohejing Town to petition Municipal Council Member Yang Xinzheng. For a time, men, women, old, and young, formed groups of no less than two hundred people. The district head and others explained the above situation, stated their intention, and requested to be accompanied to the Land Bureau to petition. Municipal Council Member Yang explained in public that the Land Bureau was acting on orders in this land acquisition. Since you have already petitioned the Ministry of Interior, you can wait quietly for instructions. Why bother wasting your work to make a pointless request? I do not approve of this. He repeatedly enlightened and persuaded the masses to return, promising to discuss appropriate solutions with the authorities. At five o'clock, the farmers finally returned.

Fishing Construction Fee Collection Method Revised; Value-Based Levy, Paid by the Seller; Fisheries Bureau Issues Public Notice Protecting Fishing Yesterday 127

The Oceanic Fisheries Administration of the Ministry of Industry in the Jiangsu-Zhejiang region, as the fishing season is approaching, besides ordering its affiliated naval vessels, including the Biao Hai, Hai Jiu, Hai Jia, Qing An, and Hai Ying, to set off to protect the fishing in different areas, discovered extortion by bandits. Yesterday, they issued a special public notice to fishermen, urging them to report such incidents to nearby naval vessels for detention. The public notice stated, "Public Notice: Now that the fishing season has arrived, it has been found that unscrupulous bandits are secretly extorting fishing boats with bandit business cards. Such illegal behavior should be severely apprehended to quell the banditry. Therefore, this public notice is hereby issued, urging all fishermen to be aware that if they encounter bandits who dare to extort fishing boats again, they may immediately secretly report them to the naval vessels of this bureau for detention and strict punishment. Let each be informed of this. Director Yuan Lianghua, November 1st, Year 12 of the Republic of China." Furthermore, the Ministry of Industry, due to the numerous obstacles encountered in the collection of fishery construction fees, specially revised the existing collection regulations. In the past, the buyer paid the fees. Now, the seller pays the fees, and the levy is changed to 2% of the value, an increase of 10%. The matter of collecting fees in Shanghai is currently under mediation.

British-American Tobacco Factories Resume Work Yesterday Morning; Labor and Management Terms Awaiting Arbitration 129

The labor dispute at the No. 1 factory of British-American Tobacco Company in Pudong, involving over 3,000 workers, has not been resolved for half a month. The Fourth District Cigarette Industry Workers' Union has submitted a request to the Municipal Government for arbitration. At the same time, they received instructions from the Municipal Party Headquarters, ordering the branch office of the British-American Tobacco Factory to order all workers to resume work first and await resolution. The Union then relayed the order to the branch office of the British-American Tobacco Factory. After receiving the order, the branch office immediately convened an emergency meeting of member representatives to discuss the resumption of work. They resolved: (1) to comply with the orders of the higher authorities and notify all workers to reluctantly resume work from tomorrow; (2) to submit all labor and management terms to the Municipal Fourth District Cigarette Workers' Union for submission to the Municipal Government for arbitration; (3) to issue a declaration of resumption of work to clarify the truth to all sectors; (4) to send representatives to negotiate with the management on the resumption of work matters. At 7:00 AM yesterday, all the workers gathered at the factory gate. Zhou Xuexiang, a member of the General Labor Union, and representatives of the Fourth District Cigarette Workers' Union persuaded them. At 9:00 AM, all the workers entered the factory to resume work. The order was quite good.

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Requests Again to Expedite Import Tax on Foreign Rice; If Delayed Further, Farmers Will Find It Even More Difficult to Survive 130

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce telegraphed both the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry yesterday, urging them to expedite the import tax on foreign rice. The original text stated, "To the esteemed Ministry of Finance and Ministry of Industry in Nanjing: We have investigated that the domestic late rice crop has already entered the market, but foreign rice continues to be dumped at low prices. It is reported that the small-grain rice sold in Fujian Province, including the province's rice tax of one yuan per *shi*, is only sold for six yuan and eighty-five cents. This will increasingly crowd out domestic grain, until it is no longer able to survive. Since the rumor of a famine last year stirred up society, public opinion at the time strongly advocated levying heavy import taxes on foreign rice. It was only because of objections from rice merchants in Guangdong Province that the authorities, for the sake of prudence, postponed implementation. Fortunately, Guangdong first created a foreign rice tax, and the resistance has been removed. If there is further delay, the decline in this year's agricultural production will inevitably be even worse than last year, and farmers will find it even more difficult to survive. We do not avoid presumption and telegraph to your departments for your review and approval, humbly requesting that the import tariff on foreign rice be implemented immediately to alleviate the suffering of Jiangsu farmers for the public good. Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce."

Japanese Minister Actively Lobbying for Renewal of Sino-Japanese Tariff Agreement; After Termination of Agreement, Japanese Goods Exported to China Plunged; Dropped from First to Third Place; Japanese Circles Currently in Great Panic 131

The Xinxin News Agency reports that, according to a Japanese newspaper yesterday, since the Sino-Japanese Tariff Agreement expired in May of this year, the Chinese government has not continued to sign with the Japanese side. On the one hand, the new tariff regulations have been implemented, resulting in a great blow to Japanese goods exported to China in the past six months, with a very large impact. Therefore, Japanese banking and business circles are quite uneasy. They all believe that this matter is related to the lifeline of Japanese commerce. Therefore, Japanese Minister to China Arichi Akira has repeatedly gone to the capital to meet with Wang Jingwei, President of the Executive Yuan of the National Government, to request continued signing, etc. A Xinxin News Agency reporter has learned from relevant sources that Japanese goods exported to China used to account for the first place in imported goods from various countries. Since the Sino-Japanese Tariff Agreement was terminated, our country, in order to protect domestic products, has implemented an autonomous tariff policy. Japanese goods exported to China have been treated as goods from non-treaty countries. As a result, the current import of Japanese goods has dropped from the first to the third place. Therefore, Japanese circles are in great panic, fearing that if this is prolonged, the situation will inevitably be unbearable. Therefore, they are actively lobbying our National Government, hoping to achieve the objectives of the agreement and restore the original state of Japanese goods exported to China. However, it is learned that the authorities of our government are well aware of the advantages and disadvantages and have long decided to adhere to the autonomous policy, not showing any retreat from any enticement or threat, and choosing their own destruction.

Illegal Recruitment Agency Busted in Nanshi 132

The Central News Agency reports that recently, in Nanshi, there have been cases of people impersonating military officers and establishing recruitment agencies to privately recruit new soldiers, which is illegal. Dispute Between Sanshan Guildhall and Cooperative Association 133

The Sanshan Guildhall sent a letter to this newspaper stating, "Dear Editor, I have read the full text of the facts announced by the Cooperative Association in your newspaper. The announcement is grandiose and designed to dazzle people, but in fact, it is far from the truth. Our guildhall does not want to remain silent, and we are hereby submitting a letter of rebuttal, hoping that it will be published in your newspaper to clarify the truth. On September 21st of this year, the National Goods Introduction Center entrusted the Yongshengtai Customs Brokerage Firm to load sixteen pieces of cloth onto the Yihe Steamship Company's Jiesheng Steamer to the Suzhou Branch. Subsequently, the brokerage firm telegraphed Fuzhou, prohibiting the consignee from picking up the goods, saying that our guildhall had ordered the brokerage firm to obstruct the goods by telegram, etc. The key elements of an order are coercion and intimidation. Yongshengtai has the freedom to operate, and there is no specific contract with our guildhall. It took the initiative to send a telegram to return the goods. How can it be called an order? Even if the firm complied with our guildhall's request and sent a telegram, it was simply like a rabbit mourning for a fox, unable to bear to see the colleagues of our guildhall being oppressed by capitalists and going bankrupt, making an unjust cry. Furthermore, on October 23rd, the National Goods Introduction Center entrusted the Sanbei Public Freight Company to transport 131 pieces of cloth, which were loaded by Sanbei Freight Company. However, the announcement stated that the Sanbei Company stated that it could not be loaded without the permission of the Sanshan Guildhall, etc. After investigation by our guildhall, the center used altered customs documents to falsely declare and transport the goods, which was discovered and rejected by the Sanbei Company. However, the announcement claimed that the Sanbei Company was coerced by the Sanshan Guildhall to refuse to load the goods. What a clever trick of embellishing words and covering up faults! The facts are all there and can be verified without difficulty. Since the center claims to introduce national products, its sole aim is to guide the people to enjoy using national goods, to widely introduce them so that the industry strives to manufacture and the business circles strive to purchase and sell, and everyone enthusiastically purchases and uses them. However, the center is not trying to do this, but instead invests in purchasing goods that are already selling well and transports them to areas where they are already widely used, so that the industry has nothing to strive for, the business circles have nowhere to strive, and the seekers have no power to purchase. Looking at what is stated in its announcement, 16 pieces of cloth were loaded to Fuzhou on September 21st, and 131 pieces of cloth were loaded to Fuzhou on October 22nd. These cloths had already been promoted and sold by the colleagues of our guildhall for many years and had a long-standing reputation, without the need for the center's introduction. The industry is only continuing what it already does, and the business circles will eventually lose their jobs. Moreover, in various parts of Fujian, the residents are thrifty and simple and have always loved using national goods. Since the 19th Route Army was stationed there, they have long implemented a policy of only using national products. The National Goods Introduction Branch was established this year, while the colleagues of our guildhall have been purchasing and selling national goods for many years. It uses the name of national goods introduction in name, while we use the name of national goods sales in practice. Now, it is introducing in name and profiting in practice, competing with the colleagues of our guildhall in business, not hesitating to slander people with destroying national goods, inciting hatred and fishing for profit, accusing people of illegal oppression, and provoking discord. Examining the center's achievements, the goods are limited to fast-selling cloth, the area is limited to Fuzhou, where national goods are actively purchased. The reality of national goods introduction is completely lacking. It has already made merchants in Shanghai and Fujian sigh for lack of food. In the future, if they continue to follow their original intention and rely on their financial strength to compete with merchants in various industries in various places for a day's advantage, national goods manufacturers will not need new development, the people will not have new knowledge, and merchants who rely on buying and selling for a living will be successively unemployed, and there is even a risk of bankruptcy. This is not the fault of national goods introduction, but the fault of using national goods introduction in name to take away people's jobs in practice. Before leaving, I feel indignant and implore you to allow publication so that those who are scheming will not hide the shortcomings of others to show the evil of their strengths, and the propaganda will be deceived, then I will be fortunate. This is addressed to the Shen Bao Newspaper Office, attached with a reply to the National Goods Production and Sales Cooperative Association. (Note: See a brief report by a Japanese reporter on the Fuzhou Sanshan Guildhall, dated October 31st)."

The China National Goods Production and Sales Cooperative Association sent a letter to the Sanshan Guildhall stating, "Dear Editor, we have received and respectfully read your reply. Regarding the various sections on monopoly and illegal obstruction of transportation, your guildhall has denied them. Our association's duty is to promote national goods and strive to develop the industry to save the country. All those who advance towards this goal are our friends, and all those who unreasonably destroy it are our enemies. The situation of your guildhall's obstruction of national goods is clear to everyone. Our association does not want to waste any more paper and ink and redo a pointless argument. However, the facts are where they are, how can they be concealed? Now, we will further explain the truth of the matter. (1) Regarding the matter of ordering the Yongshengtai Customs Brokerage Firm to send a telegram to Fuzhou to prevent the pick-up of goods, when the firm was forced to send the telegram, the Yihe Shipping Bureau, fearing legal issues, ordered the firm to issue a formal document, which is now stored at the shipping bureau and can be used as evidence. Also, on that day, the Yongshengtai Customs Brokerage Firm was acting as an agent for the Meisheng Customs Brokerage Firm in re-reporting the agency transport. Upon receiving a telegram from Fuzhou reporting the stoppage of delivery, our association immediately interrogated the firm, ordering it to truthfully reply. Subsequently, it approved a letter stating that Yongshengtai said that it was because the Introduction Center had not joined the Fuzhou Cotton Cloth Gang Sanshan Guildhall, so the guildhall interfered with the customs firm and needed to return the goods. Our association exists, so how can your guildhall deny knowing? The Yihe Shipping Bureau also has a statement regarding this case, which is also available to our association. (2) Regarding the Sanbei Company's refusal to transport, the company's manager Yu formally stated to the Introduction Center's manager Shi that he could not issue a customs declaration without the permission of Mr. Wang of the Sanshan Guildhall. What can your guildhall say in defense? (3) Regarding the refusal to load the China Merchants Bureau steamer, what do you mean by 'passive self-defense'? What kind of oppressive behavior did the China Merchants Bureau engage in that made your guildhall have to defend itself? This is truly what is meant by trying to cover up the truth, and yet you still say that it is not contrary to the law or reason? With this, we respectfully wish you good health. China National Goods Production and Sales Cooperative Association, November 1st."
