Letter from the Taxpayers' Association to the Public Works Department 137

Dear Editor, we have received the letter from the 20th District Branch of the Shanghai Citizens' Federation and the United Business Association of the Fourth District on October 14th, stating that since the electricity strike in the Public Concession occurred, all sectors have been uneasy. It is like what US President Roosevelt recently said to capitalists in his country, "Only see your own interests and disregard people's lives." There is a growing trend to force expansion, because what the company authorities see is only profit, and the chairman of the Chinese Chamber of Commerce is not even in their eyes, let alone our suffering Chinese workers. Your association's letter to the Public Works Department, requesting it to control them, is righteous and stern, revealing the hidden and exposing the covered, and it is truly admirable. This is indeed a true representation of the residents within the boundary. Last night and this morning, the Shanghai Electric Power Company published a public letter in the newspapers at a huge cost. On the surface, it seems that the company is reasonable in everything, not only is there nothing right about the workers, but also the opinions of public organizations, such as the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce's declaration and your association's letter, are also considered to be inaccurate, untrue, or intended to confuse observers. It is truly like what is said in the New Testament, "Only see the speck in other's eyes, but not see the log in your own eyes." Our association is not talented, but dares to refute each of its points separately in order to correct the audience. We inform your association: (1) Regarding the electricity price of the Shanghai Electric Power Company, the exclusive agreement stipulates that the original electricity price set by the Public Works Department's Electricity Department should be regarded as the most fair price, and should gradually be reduced in the future. The price increase began on January 1st of last year. The reason was that the price of coal was high. Now, the price of coal has been reduced by half, and it is being dumped, almost half of what it was when the price increase was requested. Then should the Electric Power Company, which uses Japanese coal, not request a price decrease? The price increase is only 3.6%, which is really deceiving. Try asking if adding one cent to a penny is equal to adding 9.09%. Why say only 3.6%? With just this one point, the company's letter has lost its authenticity. It is also said that the wages of Chinese employees have increased by 2.06%. Then the company has made a comparison as follows: (A) The original income was 10 million tons, plus 3.6%, which is 360,000 taels. (B) The original expenditure on wages was 100,000 taels, plus 20.6%, which is 20,600 taels. It is sufficient to prove that electricity prices and wages cannot be compared with each other. (2) This article does not need to be debated in detail. Just look at the company's use of White Russians, which is enough to see the falsity of what it says. Proving that the monthly salary of foreigners is more than 100,000 taels, while that of Chinese is only more than 10,000 taels, is even more difficult to believe. (3) Regarding bonuses, those who are fired are not given them, and those who resign are not given them. Consider that there are only two ways for workers to leave the company, and yet they are not given bonuses. Then the bonuses in words and orally, no matter how great, are no different from empty promises. (4) The accuracy of the meter reading is only a one-sided statement. It must be like the mint's production of coins and the bank's banknotes, organizing a public committee to review them before people can fully believe them. As for the lawsuits for stealing electricity, they still come from the teachings of your association. Try asking if the power outage to our member Lao Yan Maoyuan, which caused the closure of his business, was a court decision? In general, the so-called true evidence of the company is only one-sided before a permanent review committee is established. The matter concerns public interests. We urge your association to continue to urge the Ministry to intervene from the standpoint of all taxpayers and not allow the words of the aforementioned Roosevelt to continue to be an iron fact. Sincerely wishing you public friendship, etc., we respond to your bureau and handle the case together.

Jardine Matheson Stevedore Workers' Union Club and Seamen's Union Suspend Activities 140

According to Xin Sheng News Agency, the wage dispute of the Jardine Matheson stevedore workers is difficult to resolve due to the refusal of various compradors to sign. The Seamen's Union believes that there is a background to the workers' slowdown, so it has suspended the activities of the Jardine Matheson Stevedore Club and dismissed the instigating staff. The details are as follows:

Deadlock Between the Two Sides: The Jardine Matheson stevedore workers launched a slowdown at the end of last month due to their unfulfilled demands for improved treatment. Subsequently, the Preparatory Committee of the Chinese Seamen's Union submitted the matter to the company for negotiation. The company accepted the three conditions put forward by the workers, and all the workers immediately resumed work. However, the dispute broke down again due to the refusal of various compradors to sign. After the seamen's branch and others tried their best to suppress the situation, the slowdown was not repeated. The last mediation convened by the Social Bureau failed to proceed due to the absence of the labor representatives. The two sides are currently still in a deadlock.

Club Sealed Off: The Preparatory Committee of the Chinese Seamen's Union recently learned that after the deadlock in the Jardine Matheson stevedore workers' wage issue, Wang Zhifu, a standing committee member of the Jardine Matheson Club, secretly colluded with the compradors, intending to betray all the workers. In order to protect the interests of the workers, the committee decided the day before yesterday (the 1st) to dismiss Wang Zhengfu, seal off the club, and prohibit its activities, and to negotiate with the Chinese Shipping Mutual Aid Association on a regular basis.

Dismissal of Staff: The Seamen's Union also believes that the stevedore workers' slowdown was instigated by Zeng Shanren, a member of the staff council, which is considered to be in violation of the law. Therefore, the union dismissed him and notified its subordinates. The original text reads as follows: "Notice: Zeng Shanren, a cadre of this union, instigated the stevedore workers of Jardine Matheson to stage a slowdown and secretly sent a letter to the company to threaten them, the evidence is conclusive. In addition to submitting the matter to the 14th committee meeting of this union for a decision to dismiss him, he will not be allowed to engage in activities within the scope of this union in the future, in order to punish him and avoid further incidents. In addition to issuing separate orders, this order is issued to inform all subordinate associations."

Yesterday, the Shanghai General Office of the World Red Swastika Society received Xu Lisheng and other representatives from Haimen for disaster relief. The government's disaster relief has not been taken into account, and no investigations have been conducted. Now that the cold winter is approaching, the disaster victims are waiting to be rescued. They are begging for funds for disaster relief and attaching a disaster relief appeal. It reads as follows: "Our Haimen eastern part is low-lying, bordering the Yellow Sea to the east,毗 Dong to the south, and connecting to the Tonghai Kenmu Company to the north. On September 2nd and September 18th of this autumn, we suffered two hurricanes, with torrential floods pouring in. Cotton, beans, miscellaneous grains suffered heavy losses, especially the stone dikes, cement dikes, and cement and wooden sluice gates along the north and south Yellow Sea coast were destroyed, and their losses are even more severe. If you want to store fresh water outside the圩 and plant inside the圩, you must first rush to repair the圩 to be the fundamental plan. Also, our western Haimen, along the Yangtze River line, east to Qidong and west to Nantong, suffered the same disaster, destroying 圩 dikes and houses, and drowning people, slightly similar to the coast. According to the survey, the affected area along the coast is about 137,600 mu, more than 2,240 houses collapsed, more than 8,400 embankments were breached, more than 140 people were drowned, and the loss of grain was more than one million yuan. More than 20,000 disaster victims are waiting for relief. High Court Rules No Need to Transfer Communist Suspect Case; Presiding Judge Orders Police to Detain Suspects for 24 Hours; Public Security Bureau and Municipal Council to Negotiate Administratively 145

The Public Security Bureau previously arrested four communist suspects, Chen Yuxiu, Xie Xinming, Xu Jian, Xie Zuoyu, and others, at No. 45 Dalu New Village, Shigaota Road. However, the police station on Dixiwei Road detained Chen and others and sent them to the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court because Shigaobei Road, which the Public Security Bureau passed through, was an extra-territorial road. The dispute over jurisdiction between the two sides was intense. Some time ago, Judge Yu of the Second Branch of the High Court visited Dalu New Village in person to investigate the situation. All the details have been recorded in our newspaper. Yesterday morning, the case was scheduled for continued hearing. At 10:00 a.m., Judge Yu Hua of the Criminal Division, accompanied by two prosecutors, Zhou Han and Jiang Shuzi, ascended to the Criminal Division One court. Li Zhishan and Gan Jingxian, lawyers for the Municipal Council, Zhan Jifeng, legal counsel for the Public Security Bureau, and Yue Junying, the defendant's defense lawyer, were all present. First, lawyer Zhan Jifeng stated that the most important jurisdictional issue in this case, which this lawyer believes, has been investigated by your court in person. It should be clear whether Dalu New Village is in the Chinese or Concession area. The defendant and others founded the Chinese-language Xinbao in Batavia, which contains many reactionary articles. The Batavia Party Headquarters petitioned the Central Government to issue an arrest warrant. Therefore, the defendant's criminal behavior is obvious. He then presented the Xinbao and other evidence. Judge Yu declared that the jurisdictional issue should be resolved first today, and the evidence can be submitted later. Lawyer Zhan immediately asserted that Dalu New Village was indeed in the Chinese area. Lawyer Li Zhishan also stated that Shigaobei Road is currently under the administration of the Municipal Council Police Department before a solution has been reached by the diplomatic authorities. Dalu New Village is a dead-end lane. If the Public Security Bureau is to perform its duties, it must pass through this road. Therefore, your court has jurisdiction. Even if it is determined that it is indeed in the Chinese area, according to the law, the Jiangsu High Court should request an arrest warrant. If the court believes that the jurisdictional issue must wait for a solution by the diplomatic authorities, then it should order the release of the defendant. Lawyer Zhan then replied that the land of Dalu New Village is outside the extra-territorial road. The tap water, electricity, and building permits of the village are all supplied and issued by the Chinese authorities. There is no doubt that it is in the Chinese area. The police station's lawyer said that the Suzhou High Court should request the transfer of the case and the Public Security Bureau has no right to request it, which is wrong. If this is the case, then the Public Security Bureau can be abolished. The Municipal Council argues that since the exit of Dalu New Village must pass through the extra-territorial road of the Concession, the Municipal Council can manage it accordingly. Then, the location of the City Chamber of Commerce is surrounded by the Concession on all sides. Whether it is the front or back door, it must cross the Concession. Why does the Municipal Council have no right to manage it? Moreover, there has never been such a road in the Yangjingbang regulations. Lawyer Li then attacked the Public Security Bureau for not following the provisions of the Criminal Procedure Law, first issuing an arrest warrant or search warrant from the court. He cited various legal provisions as the reason for his attack. Lawyer Zhan immediately stated that the Public Security Bureau's arrest of the defendant was in accordance with the orders of the superiors. If the procedure is indeed inconsistent, the higher authorities will correct it themselves, and the Municipal Council does not need to overstep its authority. The two sides debated each other. The jurisdictional issue was debated for quite some time. Judge Yu then announced that the court would adjourn for deliberation. After deliberation, he still took the seat and announced the ruling in the main text: "Chen Yuxiu, Xie Xinming, Xu Jian, and Xie Zuoyu are not criminals found in the Public Concession. This court does not need to transfer them. The bail money is returned." After the ruling, Lawyer Zhan immediately stated that the court had ruled that the defendant was not a criminal found in the Public Concession, but was forcibly detained by the Municipal Council. Now that your court has the right to accept the case, I am deeply afraid that the police station will release him. Then, the important criminal will escape. Who will be responsible? Therefore, at a minimum, the police station must detain the defendant and send him back to Dalu New Village to restore the original state. However, the Municipal Council disputed this again. Finally, Judge Yu verbally announced that the police station should temporarily detain the defendant for 24 hours, and the Public Security Bureau and the Municipal Council should conduct administrative negotiations to seek a solution. If a solution cannot be found within the time limit, the defendant should be sent back to Dalu New Village to restore the original state. However, it is heard that the Municipal Council will execute the ruling.

Another Criminal Apprehended in Bank Robbery Case; Niu Anhe Also Involved in Murder and Other Cases 146

At dusk on October 15th, 1929, a few robbers suddenly drove a car to the back gate of the British Bank on the Bund No. 6 when the market was closing. They got out of the car and rushed into the bank, broke into the accounting room. Two robbers each held a pistol, frightening and prohibiting the staff from speaking out. The remaining robbers stole an iron box, took it away, and fled in the original car. Afterwards, the bank reported that the box contained 1,052 taels of silver and 9600 yuan, all of which were lost. They reported to the police station and requested investigation. It has been five years since then, and the robbers in this case have not been completely arrested and punished according to the law. It was not until last month that Liu Junqing, the deputy detective of the Laozha Police Station, learned that the robber Niu Ziping (also known as Niu Anhe) from Anhui Province was hiding in Meitan Street, Nanjing. He immediately rushed there and requested the assistance of the local military police to arrest Niu and bring him to Shanghai for interrogation. According to the investigation, Niu Anhe is the younger brother of Anru. Anru was previously suspected of being involved in the assassination of former Finance Minister Song and was arrested by the Municipal Public Security Bureau. However, he escaped from prison. In addition to being involved in the robbery of a huge sum of money from the British Bank, Anhe also gathered a group in Sanyuanfang, Yangshupu Road on August 22, 1928, to beat Gu Bao from Guangdong Province to death and injure Wu Biao. One of the accomplices in the case, Dai Feiyun, was arrested and sentenced to imprisonment. Currently, Ru Baoyi, a lawyer from the Municipal Council Legal Group, has filed a lawsuit against Niu based on the investigation, requesting that he be punished for robbery and intentional injury causing death. Yesterday morning, he was escorted to the First Special District District Court, and presiding judge Feng Shide interrogated him. First, lawyer Ru stated the case, and then Fei Zhenyong, the accountant of the British Bank, testified about the robbery that day. When questioned, the defendant also confessed. Judge Feng then ordered the defendant to be remanded in custody and rescheduled the hearing.

Two Kidnappers Executed by Firing Squad; Serial Offenses of Kidnapping for Large Sums; Death Penalty Executed Yesterday 147

The kidnappers Gao Changsheng and Ma Qiaosheng, etc., colluded to kidnap the rice merchant He Jiechun in January 1931, extorted a large sum of money for their own use. He's relative Zhu Qirong, was found to be a wealthy businessman due to his negotiation of the ransom, so they planned to kidnap him as well. At the same time, they planned to kidnap Shen Mengyi, etc., and also robbed the jewelry of the prostitute Hong Juhua. They were notorious repeat offenders. They were arrested by the Concession police and sent to the First Special District Court, which sentenced them to death. After submitting the case to the Provincial Government for approval, they were executed by firing squad. At 10:00 a.m. yesterday, a judge from the Special Court opened the court to verify the identities of the criminals. He then ordered the police to transfer the criminals to the execution ground of the First Prison in Caohejing. Wu, a prosecutor appointed by the Shanghai District Court, led police chief Chen Junfang, police officer Chen Xihui, and execution police officers Wang Jianqing and Zhu Zhiqi to the execution ground. According to Gao Changsheng's confession, he was 25 years old, from Zhenjiang, and used to drive a car. He requested that his mother be notified to collect his body. Ma Qiaosheng confessed that his other name was Qiaosheng, he was 30 years old, from Wuxi, and used to be a servant. He asked that his wife be notified to collect his body. There were no other last words. The official ordered the execution by firing squad. The bodies were collected and sealed, and the family members collected them.

At 10:00 a.m. yesterday, a bizarre and tortuous case of massive fraud occurred at Kuangjia Company, Hejia Lane, Shangwen Road, Xiaoximen. He had studied at Kuangcun Middle School since he was a child and had just now

Because of the friendship between relatives, he came to pay a special visit while passing through Shanghai. Kuang listened to him and thought that there was no Kuang Bin in his clan. Mr. Chu Minyi 154

Pudong Bloodshed: Thugs Kill Mother and Daughter; Dying Wife of Hu Cries Out, "Number Ten Killed Me!" Neighbor Yu Lianshan Detained as Suspect 159

Regarding the case of three thugs who suddenly arrived at the home of Hu Changming, a resident of Maoye Lane, Lujia Residence, Pudong, around 10 p.m. the night before last, first robbing and then killing Hu's daughter with a key and injuring Hu's wife, which was reported in yesterday's newspaper, we have learned that Hu's wife, Yu, has also died from her serious injuries. Further details are as follows:

Opening Fire After Robbery: The night before last, when the thugs broke into Hu's house, Hu was already sound asleep. Hu's wife, Yu, was sitting in the room chatting with her niece, Chen Yu, leaving only Hu's daughter, Xiuzhen, doing chores outside the room. The thugs immediately tied her hands and feet with rope and snatched a gold-plated ring from her hand before shooting her dead. Then, they rushed into the room and took a gold-plated ring from Hu's wife and four gold-plated rings and a gold-plated bracelet from Chen Yu's hand. They also found 200 yuan in silver notes hidden away. At that moment, Hu's wife was also shot and fell to the ground. Hu had already been awakened and, seeing the criminals with weapons, dared not get out of bed to resist. Only after the criminals fled did he and his niece come out of the room, only to see his beloved daughter lying in a pool of blood. Although Hu's wife was unconscious at this time, she still had a faint breath, so he ordered people to take her to the Pudong Hospital. The hospital, seeing the severity of her injuries, urgently administered a life-saving injection. She gradually regained consciousness and cried out, "Number Ten killed me!" She repeated this twice before fainting again. She was then sent to the Shanghai Hospital in the Nanshi district for treatment.

Bodies of Mother and Daughter Inspected: Yesterday morning, Xie Along, the head of the 24th district, filed a report with the local court requesting an inspection of the body of Hu's daughter. Unexpectedly, Hu's wife also died in the hospital at 10 a.m. due to her serious injuries. Hu sent someone to carry the body back to his home in Pudong. In the afternoon, the court appointed Prosecutor Wu to cross the Huangpu River to Pudong and inspect the bodies of the mother and daughter. The onlookers were deeply saddened. The judge determined that the deceased had both died from gunshot wounds. Just as he was about to return, Hu suddenly rushed to the judge, knelt down, and kowtowed several times, loudly proclaiming his grievance. Prosecutor Wu ordered Hu to first prepare coffins and place the two bodies separately, and then report to the court for questioning tomorrow (i.e., today).

Neighbor Yu Lianshan Detained: When this case occurred, Chief Zhang of the Third District initially suspected it was a robbery. However, after hearing that Hu's wife had cried out before her death that "Number Ten" had killed her, he believed there might be a clue to follow. According to the victim Hu Changming, "The 'Number Ten' my wife mentioned, I suspect, is a certain person who used to be a patrolman with the number ten. This person now works elsewhere. Previously, Yu Lianshan, my neighbor from Qingjiang across the street, had asked me to betroth my daughter to this patrolman, but I refused. Now that I am old and have no son, I have hired a matchmaker to find a son-in-law. It is possible that this patrolman holds a grudge and committed this act." He also said, "When I held a banquet, Yu Lianshan also came to eat and complained at the table. After the incident, Yu behaved suspiciously. In reality, Yu and the murderer are likely colluding. I request his detention for investigation." The District Chief found Hu's statements to be quite reasonable and immediately detained Yu Lianshan for strict interrogation. However, Yu insisted that he had not conspired to commit murder. The District Chief ordered him to be detained in the district pending the arrest of the "Number Ten" patrolman he mentioned, after which further questioning would be conducted.

Ministry of Finance Issues Notice Strictly Prohibiting the Private Production of Counterfeit Cigarettes and Tax Evasion 161

The Ministry of Finance issued a notice yesterday, stating: "For the strict enforcement of prohibitions and earnest admonishments, it has been observed that handmade cigarettes often counterfeit the trademarks of various Chinese and foreign companies, selling them privately and evading taxes. This not only encroaches on the market for machine-made cigarettes and harms the business of legitimate tobacco merchants but also results in significant losses to the national tax revenue. According to laws and tax regulations, this is strictly prohibited. Considering the livelihood of the poor, it was not deemed appropriate to prohibit it outright. Instead, inspections and investigations were ordered, with penalties imposed for cases of violation. The Taxation Administration was also instructed to separately formulate single-item measures for the taxation of handmade cigarettes, which have been reviewed, approved, and promulgated. The tax rate is specially reduced compared to machine-made cigarettes, which is considered compassionate. However, recent investigations have revealed that many handmade cigarette producers are still privately producing counterfeit cigarettes and selling them in the market. In particular, the area near the tobacco-producing regions of southern Henan and northern Anhui is flooded with illegal cigarettes, which is blatantly audacious. Even in Ningbo in Zhejiang and Liuhe in Jiangsu, there have been repeated seizures in recent days. This has led to widespread emulation, and the situation is worsening. It has also been heard that local people's organizations are even engaging in private protection. Such pursuit of profit is blinding, and the disregard for laws and regulations is deeply regrettable. The complete prohibition of handmade cigarettes, strict investigation, search, and arrest should have been immediately implemented to rectify the situation and purify the tax administration. However, in consideration of the livelihood of the people, it is unbearable to punish without educating. In addition to notifying the provincial governments and ordering the relevant local county governments to work with the unified tax agencies and local military police to conduct secret investigations, strictly investigate, and punish private cigarette production, this strict prohibition is further clarified. All local cigarette producers, merchants, and people should be aware of this. You must know that counterfeiting cigarette trademarks, privately producing, and evading taxes is not only a violation of tax regulations but also a criminal offense. Once caught, you will be severely punished and sentenced according to the law. You must wake up from your past mistakes, follow the correct path, either pay taxes according to regulations, or switch to another occupation. Do not privately produce counterfeits and violate the prohibitions. All local people's organizations should especially uphold public duty, abide by the law, and not engage in private protection or self-indulgence. After this admonishment, if the aforementioned violations are found again, it will be deemed persistent and unrepentant. In order to protect customs duties and prevent private evasion, the Ministry will definitely consult and dispatch troops to strictly arrest, prosecute, and punish according to the law. Those local bullies who use local organizations as a pretext for protection will be thoroughly investigated and severely punished if the facts are verified. No leniency will be shown. Be cautious and heedful. This notice is hereby issued."

Dyeing Workers Refuse to Discuss Liquor Subsidy with the Silk Industry Reform Committee; New Standards Will Be Established for Valuation 167

The Silk and Satin Dyeing Trade Association Reform Committee of this city has been unable to resolve the dispute over the opposition of the Silk and Satin Cloth Office to disrupting the liquor subsidy agreement and the demand to separate the liquor subsidy and the work stoppage for ten days. The Reform Committee replied to the silk industry's request to separate and restore dyeing prices, but the silk industry seems unable to accept the Liu Kai issue. If dyeing prices are restored, the agreement can be fulfilled. Yesterday, the Reform Committee sent another letter to the silk industry. The original letter is recorded below:

"Responding to your letter of the 2nd of this month, we have learned everything. Our association has experienced a work stoppage due to the labor's request to separate the liquor subsidy. This liquor subsidy is included in the dyeing price agreement and is part of the dyeing price paid by your industry. Whether it is mixed or separated, it seems to have an impact on the basis of the dyeing price agreement. The labor's request for separation is purely to maintain the economic independence of the workers and to prevent future disputes between labor and management. Their attitude is firm. Your association's response regarding the separation of the liquor subsidy is that it is difficult to change due to the restrictions of laws and contracts and that there is no room for maneuvering. In order to avoid further escalation of the situation, our association has again sought solutions from the labor. Regarding the dyeing price agreement signed by the Municipal Government Bureau of Agriculture and Commerce sixteen years ago and the new product crepe price regulations continued in the nineteenth year, we request that your association strictly order your members to abide by them and fulfill the agreement. Now, there are also newly invented Hua Jin crepe and various crepe products with long lengths that urgently require new prices to match the cost. Some silk companies deduct dyeing prices, and dyeing shops violate contracts and disrupt prices. Both sides should earnestly correct these issues to maintain business. Our association has decided to send representatives to your office at 2 p.m. on the 5th of this month to learn and discuss the dyeing prices of the aforementioned new products and long crepe, and we request that your association appoint a responsible representative to negotiate and establish standards for price settlement. Our association will have a basis to actively resolve the issue with the labor and resume work as soon as possible to quell the dispute. We hope for your reply."

Addressed to the Shanghai Silk and Satin Trade Association.

China Merchants Steam Navigation Company to Develop Maritime Transport; Sanbei Line to Add North and South Ocean Routes 168

The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's undertaking of the water-land combined transport of state-owned railways has caused opposition from all private shipping companies, who have requested the central government to allow them to participate as well. Amidst this intense dispute, the Sanbei Steam Navigation Company has plans to operate North and South Ocean routes and add new ocean liners to develop domestic transport. After many days of discussion, these plans are about to be realized. The latest news is divided as follows:

Inaugurating Qingdao Route 169

In recent years, Sanbei Steam Navigation Company has rapidly increased its number of ships and expanded its tonnage. However, its shipping business has always focused entirely on the Yangtze River. Therefore, the number of voyages and ships traveling up and down the Yangtze River is even greater than that of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company. In terms of coastal shipping, there is no dedicated route yet. Now that the company has purchased the Jingan ship from the Ministry of Navy, which has excellent passenger accommodations and can also transport goods, it is undergoing major repairs. The company's owner, Yu Qiaqing, believes that the number of passengers traveling between Shanghai and Qingdao is increasing daily, and the exchange of goods is also very crowded, mostly transported by foreign shipping lines, which is a pity as profits are flowing overseas. Also, Qingdao has a public wharf where ships can dock, eliminating the need to purchase and build one. Therefore, it is more convenient to open a route. After discussions, it was decided to implement it. Once the Jingan leaves the dock, it will immediately travel this route. This ship will run on a regular schedule to provide transportation for passengers between Shanghai and Qingdao.

Adding South China Ships 170

The company has a large number of ships and a surplus of tonnage. The larger ocean liners, such as Mingshan, Taishan, and Longyi, are all leased out. Since the boycott of Jardine Matheson in Guangdong on the South China route, the Ewo and China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's South Seas liners have been doing very well, with each voyage fully loaded. In the spring of this year, the company had already trialed a voyage to Shantou, Xiamen, and Guangdong, which was handled by Mr. Chen Shuntong of Zhongwei Company with excellent results. It has long been planned to formally dispatch ships, but it has been delayed until today due to lack of preparation. At the moment, the various merchants in South China are in need of tonnage. Sanbei Company has repeatedly contacted various passenger companies and believes that the time is ripe. It has decided to add a new route from Shanghai to Shantou, Xiamen, and Guangdong. Before the wharves and warehouses in each port have been added, passengers and cargo will temporarily be loaded and unloaded alongside the ships. The ships to be dispatched are currently being discussed and allocated. Once they are assigned, the regular schedule will be officially launched. This is also a good sign for the Chinese shipping industry.

All Navigators of China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Oppose Income Tax 171

Since August, all central government officials have been required to pay income tax, with rates ranging from 1% on incomes above 50 yuan to 8% on incomes above 700 yuan. The higher the salary, the higher the tax. This income tax is used to fund party expenses. Customs and postal workers are also required to pay it. As the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company is a state-run organization, its crew members are also required to pay it. The engineers have already petitioned for its cancellation to express their opposition. Now, all the ship captains, chief mates, and second mates of the Navigation Department have also submitted a petition to the general manager opposing the payment of income tax. The petition argues that the navigators of each ship are merely in a labor-capital relationship and do not have the qualifications of government officials or are not central government employees. According to the income tax regulations, crew members should not pay it. It also cites that although customs and postal workers belong to state-run organizations, their treatment is different from that of crew members, and there is no reason for them to pay income tax. It requests that it be immediately abolished and that the deducted amounts be returned in full. This petition was forwarded to the company by the Navigators' Association yesterday.

Bankers' Association Held Executive Committee Meeting Yesterday; Set Dates for Statutory Holidays for Next Year; Organized a Savings Law Research Committee 172

The Shanghai Bankers' Association held its 36th executive meeting at 2 p.m. yesterday. More than 20 executive committee members and bank representatives attended. The chairman was Chen Guangfu. The following issues were discussed: (1) Regarding the case of setting the bank holiday dates for the next year, it was resolved that in addition to Sundays, when businesses are closed as usual, banks will be closed for one day on National Day, three days for the Gregorian New Year, four days for the Spring Festival, one day each in summer and autumn, and two days during the semi-annual closing of accounts. No arbitrary rest is allowed outside of the prescribed times. (2) Regarding the case of how to offer opinions on the government's proposed savings law, it was resolved to first solicit the opinions of each bank, organize a research committee to study it, and tentatively appoint nine members, with Qu Jigang as the director. (3) Regarding the case of the Zhonghui Bank's request to join as a member, it was resolved to pass it. The remaining cases were brief. The meeting adjourned.

The Central Political Council resolved that the provisional expenses are for the purchase of the new prison site, which is important for the recovery of concession legal rights. It should be approved as usual and has been forwarded by the National Government to the Executive Yuan, the Supervisory Yuan, and the Directorate General of Budget, Accounting and Statistics for compliance.

Big Fire in Tangjiawan Last Night; Five City Houses Destroyed 179

At 8:45 p.m. last night, a fire broke out suddenly at Zhou Wanxing Nian Gao Shop, No. 413 Zhaozhou Road, Tangjiawan, Nanshi. In an instant, the flames spread and extended to five stores, including Ziyun Xiang Dried Bean Curd Shop at No. 411, Wang Tongchun Porridge Shop at No. 409, Kang Hou Wine Shop at No. 407, and Chunxing Hot Water Stall at No. 405. The upper floors of Nos. 413, 411, and 409 were completely destroyed, and the losses were heavier. In addition to the Chinese fire trucks that should have arrived, the French Concession Fire Brigade also drove to assist in the rescue because the road across the street from that location belonged to the French Concession Avenue Rawie. The cause of the fire is unknown. The arsonist has fled in fear of punishment. The Second District General Office is currently dispatching personnel to investigate thoroughly.

Municipal Council Did Not Approve Dance Halls Extending Hours 180

Six dance halls in the Public Settlement, represented by Price Waterhouse & Co., accountants, petitioned the Shanghai Municipal Council to extend the restriction on business hours from 1 a.m. to 4 a.m. This proposal was discussed by the Defence Committee, which deemed it inappropriate to approve. The Board of Directors reported it on the 1st of this month, and the Board of Directors rejected it. The regulations for closing doors at 2 a.m. will be strictly enforced. Prior to 1930, the regulations stipulated that these entertainment venues should close at 2 a.m., but those who paid a special fee could extend the hours to all night. In 1929, there was a strong opposition to this all-night arrangement. As a result, the Municipal Council decided to limit the hours to 2 a.m., with no exceptions except for National Day and public holidays. Later, after petitions from the owners of each venue, it was permitted to extend the hours to 4 a.m. on Saturday nights, but a special fee had to be paid. This arrangement has been implemented in consultation with the French Concession for three and a half years. According to the Commissioner of Police, there are no new reasons for this request to extend the hours. The regulations do not need to be changed. The chairman of the Defence Committee expressed his deep regret that some people stay in entertainment venues until late at night, which seriously damages their personal finances and abilities.

Famous Painter Gao Qifeng Dies 181

The famous painter Gao Qifeng came to Shanghai a few days ago to prepare for the Berlin Painting Exhibition, intending to be a representative to Germany. Unexpectedly, he caught a cold on the way, which triggered an old illness. He died at 3 p.m. on the 2nd of this month at the Dahua Hospital in this city. Mr. Gao worked hard for the revolution and had a very glorious history, but he did not dwell on his achievements and devoted himself to art. His works have been exhibited many times at domestic and foreign art exhibitions and have won praise in the art world. At the Paris art exhibition opened by Xu Beihong, twelve of the works displayed were purchased by the French government, and Mr. Gao's work was one of them. His sudden death is a great loss to our country's artists.

Restaurant Waiter Dealing Opium and Trafficking Humans – Thirteen Male and Female Criminals Arrested Last Night – Evidence Found, Handed Over to the Headquarters for Interrogation 183

Chen Qiulin, a native of Pudong, aged 35, working as a waiter at the Shenhe Restaurant opposite Little World in the city, cohabited with a woman surnamed Shen from Tongzhou Province, aged 30, residing at No. 7 Old School Yard. He routinely engaged in the private sale of opium for smoking and colluded with hooligans to lure and sell women, profiting from the illicit gains. However, the scheme was discovered by Liu Yanfang, the chief of the first district, second precinct of the Municipal Public Security Bureau. He immediately dispatched detectives Ren Shouzhi and patrol officer Zhang Panchi, along with police chief Li Fuyi and officers, who secretly went to the address around 8 PM last night. At that time, Chen Shen, the cohabitant, and Chen Qiulin were arguing and ingesting raw opium. While rescuing them, thirteen people, including smokers and men and women chatting at Chen's house, were apprehended. Upon interrogation, they all spoke evasively. Opium lamps, pipes, and red documents were found during the search. The list of names taken to the precinct is as follows: (1) Chen Qiulin (35 years old), from Pudong; (2) Chen Qiuhe (30 years old), from Pudong; (3) Chen Shen (32 years old), from Tongzhou; (4) Chen Xiaomei (16 years old), from Jingjiang; (5) Wang Zhoushi (29 years old), from Wuxi; (6) Lu Xushi (28 years old), from Taicang; (7) Huang Hongsheng (37 years old), from Pudong; (8) Yu Kaosheng (35 years old), from Sajing; (9) Gu Jinsheng (42 years old), from Pudong; (10) Jiang Aren (38 years old), from Pudong; (11) Cai Shaoji (33 years old), from Wuxi; (12) Pan Xushi (37 years old), from Pudong; (13) Huang Geng (21 years old), from Pudong. After interrogation by Chief Liu, Chen Xiaomei (16 years old), from Jingjiang, confessed that when she was eleven years old, she was betrothed to Tong Fugen from Wuxi as a child bride. However, her fiancé died of illness in the first lunar month of this year, and she was severely beaten by her grandmother. In March, she was brought to Shanghai from Wuxi and instructed to work at the Xin Shen Cotton Mill in Caojiadu. Her grandmother left, and later, Wang Zhoushi, who was also apprehended, used sweet words to deceive her and lure her to No. 18 Baoxing Lane, Dongxin Bridge, French Concession, where she stayed for three nights. She was matched with an unfamiliar 21-year-old man. He said he was doing business on a boat. They agreed on a betrothal gift of over 100 silver dollars. Today, they were taken to Chen Qiulin's house to pay the money and hand over the person, to be married the day after tomorrow, when they were arrested during a fight. Wang Zhoushi (29 years old), from Wuxi, only admitted to taking Chen Xiaomei to Little World to play. The rest of her testimony was cunning. The other people claimed they were visiting friends, and so on. Chief Liu, considering the case involved luring women for sale and operating an opium den in violation of the law, ordered the thirteen male and female criminals, along with the evidence, to be handed over to the Headquarters for legal proceedings yesterday.

Charred Corpse of a Young Child Found in Anren Street Fire 185

Head Charred and Face Disfigured – A Gruesome Sight

The Xie Xing Jade Workshop at No. 148 Anren Street, inside the New North Gate, caught fire carelessly around 5:00 PM on the 30th of last month. Fire brigades from various districts responded and extinguished the blaze, which destroyed more than twenty buildings housing over forty families. A daughter of Wang Zhao from No. 214 Yuyuan Road, named Amao, died from injuries sustained after jumping from the building. Details have been reported in this newspaper. It is now known that Chen Ziming, a 36-year-old from Suzhou who runs a leather suitcase business in Bengbu, his wife Wang, and their two daughters and one son lived at the Xie Xing Jade Workshop on the fourth floor. The eldest daughter was Jinmei, aged 14, the second daughter was Kunbao, aged 12, and the youngest was a son named Arong, who was just four years old. On the 23rd of last month, Wang went to her hometown on important business, leaving only Jinmei and the other two children to watch over the house. When the fire broke out, the flames were intense on the lower floors, burning through the staircase. The flames spread to the upper floor, filling the room with red heat. Jinmei and the others were terrified. Jinmei immediately climbed to the roof, but her younger brother Arong was too young and weak to climb. Therefore, his second sister, Kunbao, disregarded her own safety and picked up her brother, intending to carry him to the roof. However, Kunbao was a young girl and did not have the strength to do so. Moreover, her head and lips had been burned by the fire and she was in unbearable pain. She had no choice but to abandon her younger brother to the flames. Jinmei then climbed onto the roof and shouted for help. Members of the various fire brigades spotted her and immediately devised a way to climb to the roof and rescue the two girls. Kunbao was rushed to the hospital for treatment. Her injuries were minor, so after the hospital applied medication and bandages, she was discharged. Chief Liu from the First District, Second Precinct brought the two girls to the precinct for questioning. It was then learned that Arong had died in the fire. Officers were dispatched to search through the rubble around the fire scene. Around 7:00 PM in the evening, the child's body was finally found, but it was charred beyond recognition, with a ruptured abdomen and protruding intestines. Considering the matter involved loss of life, the local authorities were ordered to report to the Shanghai District Court for an autopsy yesterday. In the meantime, his family was notified to come to Shanghai to enshroud the child's body.

According to the reserve's issuance regulations, the issuance of banknotes must have full reserves, with a cash reserve of at least 60% and a guarantee reserve of no more than 40%. The 200th announcement of the Shanghai Reserve Bank on October 28, 22nd year, is recorded below: The total amount of banknotes in circulation is 25,196,437 yuan. Page 13

Free Talk

Dissenting Views on "New Discourse on Teachers" 200

— Yu Xia

Mr. Shi Zhecun has raised objections to my work, "New Discourse on Teachers," which seems to aim at dispelling heresies and rectifying people's minds. Do I enjoy arguing? No, I am compelled to do so! I also have objections to his objections.

First, I said, "Teachers are certainly not entirely worthy of respect," to make it clear that there are aspects of teachers that are worthy of respect. I also said, "Teachers are not necessarily valuable," implying that there may be aspects of teachers that are valuable. Moreover, this rationale is based on the teachings of Confucius and Mencius. Mr. Shi, an advocate of reading the Analects, should find this gratifying, and might even smile and say, "Virtue is never solitary; it is sure to have neighbors!" As for Mr. Shi saying that my article "explains in the first paragraph that teachers originally have no qualities worthy of respect," it seems that Mr. Shi got confused from reading literary selections. In fact, my intention was merely to say that teachers have aspects that are worthy of respect and aspects that are not worthy of respect, hence the statement "Teachers are certainly not entirely worthy of respect."

Second, Mr. Shi said, "We can dismiss university professors because of differences in thought and doctrine, but we can never deny the mentors of primary and secondary schools because of our own increased learning." This is the key point of Mr. Shi's article. My article does not seem to touch upon this point, so it would not be necessary to respond. Even if discussing Meng Ke's debate about teachers and students, as Mr. Shi said, "speaking for Mr. Wei," the school where Mr. Wei lived clearly had the word "special" on its sign, and the teachers in the school should be "masters" and "professors." Perhaps the reason he wanted to criticize a certain society's art exhibition was, as Mr. Shi said, "We can dismiss university professors because of differences in thought and doctrine." (If this is the case, Mr. Wei should thank Mr. Shi for offering an explanation for dismissing his teacher.) Perhaps Mr. Wei had read the Analects and believed that "the foundation of moral cultivation" is good, following the sage's teaching of "not yielding to one's teacher in the pursuit of benevolence," which is also possible.

Third, Mr. Shi, being honored as a "remnant of the Qing dynasty" and a "young rascal from the foreign concessions," humbly declined and could not avoid writing a lengthy article to defend himself. Who does not want to be good? I also sympathize. Now Mr. Shi wants to respectfully give Mr. Wei Mengke the title of "frivolous." Even if Mr. Wei is unwilling to come out and defend himself, what you do not wish for yourself, do not do to others. Confucius' consistent life philosophy is about loyalty and forgiveness. Mr. Shi must have read the Analects, as it is "the foundation of moral cultivation." I wonder what his thoughts are? Otherwise, I highly suspect that even if someone has read the Analects and solemnly advises others to read the Analects, their "moral cultivation" is still questionable.

Honestly, the main idea of my "New Discourse on Teachers" is entirely based on the old principles of Confucius, Mencius, and Han Yu. There is no "new knowledge" or "new thought" in it. The title "New" is deliberately used as a joke, and it is actually just a record and not a creation. Therefore, it will not lead to any serious "serious problem in society," unless the person who says this has ulterior motives.

Blacksmiths 201

— Hei Ying

Summer, this is a fiery pit.

The bellows roar, and when Little Pockface's hands become weak, the fire in the furnace is red and hot again; the iron bars and iron blocks are placed in the fire, and after being burned for a while, they turn red.

Then: Tat-tat-tat丨the iron hammer strikes down.

The sparks are scorching.

"Ya Biao, be careful!"

Old Chan says to Ya Biao, who is raising the iron hammer. Ya Biao, whose face and body are all very dirty, is a newcomer. He clenches his teeth, panting: this work is really hard.

Now autumn is already deep. But Ya Biao and Little Pockface are both sweating.

Zhong Laoer is using a drill; it turns with a scratching sound, and silver-like iron filings fall on the ground.

It's all turbid smoke. It's so stuffy in the shop!

The board walls are black, the floor is black, and the bed boards where they sleep are also black. But when it gets dark, they are already so tired that they don't care about anything and fall down and snore.

On this day, it is raining outside. The weather is very cold. Early in the morning, Little Pockface is puffing and pulling the bellows: once the fire is lit, it immediately warms up. Old Chan hasn't gotten up yet: Ya Biao, rubbing his sleepy eyes, walks out. He looks at the many things that need to be done, and instinctively takes a breath.

"What's wrong, Ya Biao?"

Little Pockface raises his voice and says.

Ya Biao stands by the stove fire:

"Damn it, I can't take it anymore!"

"Why?"

"Look here: I have to finish it today! Old Chan won't help, Little Pockface, I only have these two hands, right?"

He holds out his hands.

Then, he takes off a lined jacket, and the one underneath is torn. Little Pockface sees a lump of flesh bulging on his arm.

Iron blocks and iron bars are placed in the fire.

When they turn red: raise the iron hammer! Tat-tat-tat... sparks fly onto Little Pockface's body.

"Ya Biao, you're so strong!"

He shakes his newly shaved head.

There is no answer.

The rain is heavier in the afternoon. Water is surging in the low-lying areas of the road, and there are no pedestrians in the cold and quiet.

Ya Biao thinks: Why hasn't Zhong Laoer come yet? We're suffering so much, but he's sleeping with his wife...

After hammering, it is dipped into the water; with a "chī" sound, steam rises from the surface of the water. Ya Biao stops, relaxes, and wipes the sweat from his forehead with his sleeve.

Zhong Laoer comes in the rain.

"Laoer, you slept so comfortably!"

He says sourly.

Zhong Laoer pats him on the shoulder, smiling: "I'll help you today, Ya Biao, don't..."

"Damn it!"

They all laugh.

Lovesickness 202

— By Sir John Suckling, translated by Yu Dayin

Why so pale and wan, fond lover?

Prithee, why so pale?

Will, when looking well can't move her,

Looking ill prevail?

Prithee, why so pale?

Why so dull and mute, young sinner?

Prithee, why so mute?

Will, when speaking well can't win her,

Saying nothing do't?

Prithee, why so mute?

Quit, quit for shame! this will not move,

This cannot take her.

If of herself she will not love,

Nothing can make her:

The devil take her!

Who Should We Recommend It To? 203

— Chen Zizhan

Mr. Shi Zhecun suddenly had a whim, thinking that "Zhuangzi and Literary Selections" are "the foundation of literary cultivation." It seems that he doesn't need it himself, so he can only "recommend" it to others. After thinking about it, who should he "recommend" it to? Ah, I got it, "youth!" "Recommend" it to young college students? He's afraid of encountering Mr. Wu Shichang. "Recommend" it to young university professors? He's afraid of encountering Mr. Yu Pingbo. "Showing off an axe in front of Master Luban," it's just showing his ignorance! Mr. Shi thought again and said:

The youth I am referring to are those who can read Zhuangzi and Literary Selections, not just middle school students. If it is middle school students, then junior high school students are not qualified to talk about this, but a few senior high school students should be counted in.

According to Mr. Shi's words, there are not many young middle school students who must read Zhuangzi and Literary Selections. What kind of youth is Mr. Shi referring to when he says "youth who can read Zhuangzi and Literary Selections"? "Remnants of the Qing dynasty?" "Young rascals from the foreign concessions?" I am ashamed that I cannot get any "new knowledge" about "Zhuangzi and Literary Selections" from Mr. Shi's "breakthrough" article, so I also "doubt" the result of Mr. Shi's breakthrough!

A Tour of the Buddhist Kingdom (Continued) 204

— Ba Jin

丨Travel Notes 1丨

Debusha is not bad, we have passed through this place back and forth. The ground is full of sand, looking over it is a yellow expanse, connected to the hillsides at both ends. A series of footprints were left in the middle of the road. These traces are very deep. At the same time, many bamboo sieves were placed in the middle of the road, one after another, only a few steps apart. At first, I thought these were prepared for pedestrians to step on, so as to avoid people feeling strenuous when moving their steps on the sand. But later, when I got closer, I realized that these were also things used by monks for alms, and sure enough, someone threw some copper coins into them. It is indeed not easy to walk on the sand. When you put your foot down, it feels like you are sinking into the sand. When you lift your foot again, a lot of sand has already accumulated in your shoe. The sun is very hot, and the sand is steamed so hot that it is about to catch fire. Your feet cannot stay on it for a minute, otherwise the soles of your feet will be steamed. Here I had to take off my hemp shoes and walk barefoot, making a running posture, although it was strenuous, I finally walked through. An older friend admitted defeat and hired a sedan chair.

This time we did not go to visit Mount Foding. When we went back, we passed by Xianren Well, and took a ladle of cold water from the well to drink. The well is located in a ravine and is always cool. We each drank a few mouthfuls. The day before, we each drank a cup of well water at Meifu Dan Well. After leaving Xianren Well, we met two or three Taoist priests. They were chatting and walking up from the mountain. One person said: The scenery of Mount Putuo is best on Mount Foding. But we only knew it was too late. We just hadn't been to this place.

The next day, everyone prepared to leave early in the morning. The receptionist of the temple said that there was a ship leaving for Shanghai in the morning, and they would send us down the mountain before six o'clock, but there was no ship on the sea. We waited at the dock for an hour and there was still no movement. Next to the dock there is a small temple, and we went in to rest. This temple is very small, and there are often sedan chair carriers disturbing it. A monk who watched the temple was washing tinware in the hall, and he complained to us about his monotonous life. While we were talking, the sedan chair carriers were knocking on the door again, and when it was about to cause trouble, the monk took a wooden stick and went out.

We waited in this small temple until twelve o'clock, and the people from the temple brought us food. We didn't expect to have this meal. Not long after we finished eating, someone came in and said that the ship had arrived. We happily went out to look, only to realize that this was a ship from Shanghai. Friend T, who was going to Haimen, left with his mother and brothers. We asked others if there were any ships going to Shanghai, and they said that there would be one at seven or eight o'clock tomorrow morning. My friend and I cannot return to Shanghai. We had to stay in Putuo for another day. When we tiredly walked back to the temple, even the receptionist who had seen us off earlier was a little surprised. He might be happy, because the temple had earned five more dollars for nothing.

Two Brothers (17) 205

— By Maupassant, translated by Li Weike

He got up and walked towards the end of the embankment again. He felt a little better, he was satisfied because he understood the reason for his irritability, glimpsed his own hidden feelings, and discovered another self.

"So I am jealous of Zhe An," he thought in his heart. "This is indeed quite despicable, this matter! I am now certain that my guess is correct, because when I heard the news that he had inherited the inheritance, the first thing I thought of was that he would marry Mrs. Lu Zuimi. But I don't like this rational fool, this annoying virtuous young woman. Then this is a jealousy without conditions, this is simply the essence of jealousy, this is jealousy for the sake of jealousy! This matter must be paid attention to!"

He walked to the signal post that indicated the height of the water inside the dock. He struck a match and shone it on the names of the ships that had already arrived outside the port and were waiting for the next high tide to enter. Among the ships about to enter the port were steamers from Brazil, Paratha, Chile, and Japan, two Danish brigantines, a Latvian clipper, and a Turkish steamer. When he saw the words "a Turkish steamer," he was as shocked as if he had seen a "Swedish steamer": he saw in a strange dream a large ship, carrying many people with turbans and wide-legged trousers climbing on those ropes.

"I'm thinking too stupidly," he thought; "the Turkish nation is originally a nation good at sailing."

He took a few more steps forward, then stopped and stared at the bay. On the right, above the Bay of Saint-Adresse, the two electric lighthouses of Cape Heffer, like two deformed, twin Cyclopes (giants with one eye in the forehead in mythology), cast their long and strong gazes on the sea. These two parallel lines emanating from two adjacent focal points, like the huge tails of two comets, descended from the top of the coast to the bottom of the horizon along a straight and boundless slope. Secondly, on the two embankments, there were two other lights, like the children of the two giants above, indicating the entrance to the port of Havre: and over there, on the other side of the Seine, we also saw other lights, many other lights, moving or still, bright or dark, like many eyes, sometimes open, sometimes closed, those yellow, red, and green eyes of various ports, staring at the dark sea covered with ships, the agile eyes of the hospitable continent, simply relying on the unchanging and regular mechanical movements of their eyelids, we seemed to see them saying; "This is me. I am Trouville, I am Honfleur, I am Pont-Audemer." And then there was the Etretat aerial lighthouse, which stood out from all other lighthouses and made people see it as a planet from such a distance. It indicated the route to Rouen across the sandbar at the mouth of the great river.

Then, on that deep water surface, on that boundless water surface that was darker than the sky, we seemed to see some stars here and there. They trembled in the night fog, appearing small, some close together, some far apart, and also appearing white, red, and green in various colors. Almost all of these stars did not move, but occasionally a few seemed to be running; these were the lights of ships that had dropped anchor and were waiting for the tide to come in, or ships that had come from afar to anchor.

At this moment, the moon rose from behind the city; she was like a huge and sacred lighthouse, burning in the sky to guide the endless real stars.

Bill murmured, almost raising his voice, "How great it is, and we are fighting over a few small coins!"

Suddenly, very close to him, in the large and dark trench between the two embankments, a black shadow slipped past, an incredibly huge black shadow. He leaned on the granite railing and looked down, he saw a fishing boat returning to the dock, this fishing boat passed by without a sound of people, without a sound of water, without a sound of oars, only being gently pushed forward by the large brown sail that was full of sea breeze.

He thought, "If we could live on this fishing boat, how peaceful we would be!" Then, as he took a few more steps forward, he saw a person sitting at the end of the embankment.

Regulations for the Meeting of Principals of Provincial Secondary Schools in Zhejiang 207

The Zhejiang Education Department has scheduled to hold a meeting of principals of provincial secondary schools from the 8th to the 10th of this month, as previously reported. The meeting regulations are as follows: 1. The purpose of this meeting is to discuss important matters in various aspects of secondary school education, discipline, and school administration. 2. This meeting is convened by the Education Department. In addition to the mandatory attendance of all principals of provincial secondary schools, the Education Department Director will appoint the Head of the Secretariat Section, Supervisors, and Editors to attend the discussions together, and may also appoint relevant staff members to attend as non-voting participants. If the principal of a provincial school cannot attend in person, they may entrust a faculty member from their school to attend as a representative. 3. The Education Department Director will chair this meeting. If the chair cannot attend due to circumstances, they will appoint someone to act as their representative. 4. The matters to be discussed at this meeting are as follows: (1) Matters concerning the implementation of secondary school laws and regulations (2) Matters submitted for discussion by the Education Department (3) Matters proposed by each school. 5. For the convenience of discussion, this meeting may be divided into the following groups to review separately and provide information for discussion at the general meeting: Group A: Teaching, Group B: Curriculum, Group C: School Administration, Group D: Education Funding, Group E: Other. When the above groups conduct separate reviews, they may each elect a chair. 6. A general meeting of this meeting requires the attendance of two-thirds or more of the total number of people to be convened. Discussions require the approval of more than half of the number of attendees to be resolved. 7. The meeting period for this meeting is set at three days and may be extended if necessary, but the extended period is limited to two days. 8. The resolutions of this meeting will be compiled and sent to the Education Department Director for approval and implementation. 9. The meeting place for this meeting is in the Education Department. 10. These regulations are formulated and implemented by the Education Department.

French Concession Private School Federation Asks Education Bureau to Strive for Subsidies　Chinese Education Rights Should Be Equal to Westerners　General Meeting to Be Held on the 5th of This Month to Re-elect Staff 212

The Private Primary and Secondary School Federation of the French Concession of this city yesterday submitted a special report to the Municipal Education Bureau regarding the request to the French Municipal Council to allocate 20% of its total annual income to Chinese education funds, requesting that it continue to negotiate with the French authorities on the basis of reason, and scheduled a general meeting of all members to be held on the 5th of this month to re-elect executive and supervisory committee members and discuss ongoing matters. Details are recorded as follows:

Submitted to the Municipal Education Bureau, the original text states: "Our association previously believed that Chinese residents in the French Concession pay a large amount of taxes every year, but the French authorities use it for Chinese education, which is less than that used for a small number of Westerners. The obligations and rights are not commensurate, favoring them over us, and neglecting Chinese education. We once proposed that from 1933, 20% of the total annual income be allocated to Chinese education funds, giving priority to subsidizing private primary and secondary schools established in the concession, in order to expand them and accommodate Chinese children, and to seek balanced development of Chinese education and Western education, and for Chinese children and Western children to receive equal treatment. We have submitted a report to your bureau repeatedly to negotiate on the basis of reason, and have been running around and calling for help, all on file. However, time has passed, although we have heard from your director about the subsidy fees for these private schools, and the French authorities have agreed to implement them from 1934, the details of the subsidy have not yet been formally announced, like a mirage that cannot be reached. We believe that your bureau, having taken responsibility for it in the past, should strive for it in the future. We respectfully request that your bureau maintain its original intention, uphold justice, and provide strong assistance from beginning to end, and continue to negotiate with the French authorities, and must clearly announce the subsidy method, so that the subsidies for primary and secondary schools in the concession can be realized as soon as possible, so as to fulfill the concerns of developing Chinese education, and to achieve equal treatment. All requests for processing are combined in this document and submitted for review, respectfully requesting that you act as requested and strive for it quickly for public convenience."

Notice to Members: The association's notice to members regarding the convening of a general meeting states: "We respectfully inform you that, upon investigation, the first item discussed at the joint meeting of the executive and supervisory committees held by our association on the 28th of this month was the date of the members' general meeting. It was decided that the members' general meeting would be held at Juebei Vegetarian Restaurant on Songshan Road at 10:00 AM on November 5th to re-elect staff. A dinner will be held after the meeting. Those who wish to participate should bring a meal fee of one yuan. The record is on file, in addition to the official letter, a corresponding record is sent to inform you, hoping you will check and attend on time."

Philippine Overseas Chinese Basketball Team Defeats Qianghua Last Night: 45 to 43, a Difference of Two Points 221

The Philippine Overseas Chinese basketball team defeated Qianghua yesterday with a score of 45 to 43. The situation in the game was quite tense, as both sides were evenly matched, making the competition fierce. After the start, the Philippine Overseas Chinese team gained momentum and scored six consecutive points. Afterwards, the two teams were evenly matched and made their own contributions. Qianghua often lagged behind by six or seven points. At the end of the first half, the Philippine Overseas Chinese team had 27 points, while Qianghua had 20. As the second half began, the Philippine Overseas Chinese team's momentum remained strong and they scored frequently. Qianghua's guards, Wu Youliang and Lin Zequn, were unable to cover everything, and the forwards were unable to defend effectively, which led to openings. After the score reached 41 to 31, Qianghua suddenly fought bravely, with Chen Xianglong and Zhou Xuexian making contributions from time to time. In an instant, they scored seven consecutive points, showing a momentum of rapid ascent and overtaking the lead, reducing the gap to three points, making the situation even more tense. At this time, the Philippine Overseas Chinese team became more vigilant, and Xu Zeyao and Lin Dengxu took the opportunity to score two more points, making the score 45 to 38. At that time, there were still about three minutes left. Qianghua suffered this setback and wanted to turn the tide, but it was too late. Still unwilling to show weakness, they made a final struggle and scored five more points, making the score 45 to 43. The Philippine Overseas Chinese team won by two points.

Youyou Cup

Yu Tianguang Wins Championship for Three Consecutive Years; Yesterday's Final Victory Over Liang Deguang; Members' Group Also Concludes 223

The third Youyou Cup Tennis Tournament, which has been delayed due to various reasons since its start, finally concluded yesterday, which is a fortunate event. According to the results of this tournament, Yu Tianguang and Liang Deguang both tied for the lead with 26 points each. According to the rules, a best-of-three series was adopted to determine the champion. The two played the final yesterday on the club's court. Yu defeated Liang with a score of 2-0, thus Yu Tianguang won the championship for three consecutive years, which is commendable. Yesterday, Liang had many unforced errors in the first set, leading Yu to win with a score of 6-2. The second set was quite tense, with Liang once leading 5-3. However, Yu remained calm throughout and won 8-6. The Youyou Cup thus concluded with this 2-0 score.
