Special Announcement

國防與體育章淵若　全國運動大會感言　改造體育方針蒭議 232

The National Defense and Sports: Zhang Yuanruo's Reflections on the National Games, Preliminary Ideas on Reforming Sports Policies

The Fifth National Games were held this year on Double Tenth Day at the Central Stadium in the capital. The nation's elite and athletes from all directions have been in high spirits for the past ten days. In front of the late Premier, at the foot of Zijin Mountain, they displayed their skills. Central figures either offered personal experiences or hosted grand banquets with solemn enthusiasm, unprecedented in scale. However, at a time when the people are impoverished, resources are exhausted, and starvation fills the roads, the nation has spared no expense, investing a massive sum of over a million [currency] to build this long-abandoned, occasionally used Central Stadium. The direct and indirect costs for the central government and various provinces and cities participating in this grand event must amount to over a million [currency] as well. This is not merely for decoration or extravagance; it is a profound and far-reaching plan for the future of the nation.

Now, as the grand event concludes, thousands of spectators take home their lingering enthusiasm. National public opinion is unanimously expressing its sincere admiration and consolation to the athletes. It is said that the sporting achievements have broken or equaled three Far Eastern Games records and broken numerous national records, especially in track and field and swimming. However, given the current situation and the times we live in, the author humbly questions whether our nation's current sports education policy, which focuses solely on running, jumping, and chasing, is a wise choice, and whether breaking records should be the sole objective.

The misguided sports policies of the past have led to various unhealthy phenomena in sports. People have followed suit, and so-called sports have become a profession for general athletes. They are undisciplined, dissolute, and degenerate in normal times and after training. On the field, they only seek personal glory and engage in reckless fights, without self-assessment or discipline. School authorities often use underhanded tactics to buy off athletes, using them as advertisements for the school's reputation, indulging and enticing them, and treating them as rare commodities. They completely ignore the cultivation of athletes' moral character. Even worse, the relationship between athletes and educators is exactly the same as that between circus owners and their tigers, leopards, and lions, or beggars and their monkeys (see "Shaoxing, Sports Don't Forget Reading," October 18). According to police expert Ding Fubao, "In every sports meet in the East and West, many athletes develop lung diseases after strenuous competitions. Sports promotion in our country in recent years has been extremely popular, but if students have latent tuberculosis and their resistance is not strong, the disease will erupt once broken down by competitive sports. Therefore, these students can only participate in small exercises and should rest. Strenuous exercises for long periods are tantamount to constructing their own deaths." In the past, Mr. Gu Zheng from Shanghai and Mr. Xue Jianyi from Wuxi, known for their involvement in sports, both suddenly died of acute pulmonary tuberculosis. Countless unknown heroes have developed lung diseases due to strenuous exercise (see Ding's preface to his "Guide to Lung Disease," published in the October 2nd Early Morning News). These views may be biased, but if our nation's sports education could adopt the principles of universality, rationality, practicality, perseverance, moderation, discipline, and cooperation as its guidelines and as standards for evaluating achievements and judging merits, rather than focusing solely on breaking records and inciting private fights, then these unhealthy phenomena would naturally not occur.

I cite this not to say that sports can be neglected (see my "The Fighting Spirit of the Nation," published in the Current Affairs News, which proves my position). As the ancient saying goes, "As Heaven maintains vigor through movement, a gentleman should constantly strive for self-improvement." Our nation's sages have always ranked archery and horsemanship alongside ritual, music, writing, and mathematics as the Six Arts. They have also regarded courage, knowledge, and benevolence as the three pillars, considering them essential virtues. The ancient Western philosopher Plato also considered "courage" as one of the four virtues that people in his ideal state should possess. Since the Jin, Wei, and Six Dynasties, our people have been decadent and unable to recover. Given the deep weakness of our nation, promoting sports is a national policy that cannot be ignored for the purpose of revitalizing the country and seeking strength in the future.

However, promoting sports emphasizes the establishment of sound sports policies and the correction of misguided sports policies. Sports in China over the past two or three decades have only focused on schools. The objective is small and lacks an overall organization and a complete system. This has led a small number of people engaged in sports to hold onto their own narrow views, defaming each other, and failing to cooperate. At this time of foreign aggression, our nation's sports policy should expand its target audience and improve its spirit, with the revival of the nation as its foundation. We should promptly promote the easiest to popularize and most practical sports, such as swimming, weightlifting, hiking, calisthenics, and martial arts, to ensure that sports in the future are nationalized, collectivized, and militarized. On the one hand, we must avoid becoming aristocratic and Westernized. On the other hand, we must integrate martial arts with military affairs, creating the simplest, most practical, and nation-reviving Chinese sports system. Since the European War, countries around the world have had a particularly clear understanding of sports, and their objectives are also different from before. As for teaching materials and methods, they all focus on stimulating national struggle, strengthening the minds and bodies of young people and the masses, and incorporating military purposes into sports (see Cheng Qike's "The Purpose of Reviving the National Foundation Through Sports," published on October 16). Do our nation's current sports policies, the spirit of sports, and the meaning of various assessments and sports styles conform to the new trends of the modern world and meet the needs of our nation? This is what we should deeply reflect on amidst the excitement, cheers, and praise.

Since the revolution in Soviet Russia, the number of athletes nationwide increased to 800,000 in 1928, 1.1 million in 1930, 3.1 million in 1932, and suddenly increased to 6 million in 1935. This sharp increase in numbers truly indicates that sports have become integrated with the people (see the Current Affairs News, October 13). Soviet Russia calls its national games not "games" but "National Defense and Production Examination." Any young person who has one of the following two conditions: (1) possessing a specialized production skill that allows them to work tirelessly for long periods; (2) possessing a specialized and refined war skill (such as using weapons, live ammunition shooting, hand grenades, fencing, horseback riding, and sailing), will be awarded a gold medal by the government, known as the first-class athlete in the country. This has a profound impact, truly nationalizing sports for national defense and production (see the Morning Post editorial, October 22). After the war, Mussolini in Italy also regarded sports as a way to revive the nation, deeply penetrating all levels of society. Given the current precarious state of our nation and the urgency of national defense, if we continue to follow the sports methods of European and American countries, merely imitating their running, jumping, and playful techniques, using athletes' qualifications as an excuse to skip classes and avoid exams, seeking the vanity of the nation by breaking records, and collectively abandoning all of our ancestral culture, artifacts and technologies while indulging in modern superficiality and extravagance, not only will it not save our nation from poverty and weakness, but it will lead our nation to a path of decline. Education Minister Tu Shijie stated the following goals for sports at the opening ceremony: (1) To implement the idea of integrating sports and moral education, being equally responsible for the physical and moral health of students. (2) Each athlete should strive for a goal that is not romantic or degenerate, always maintaining a lofty attitude and a spirit of hard work. The President gave a speech to all the athletes, saying, "The meaning of sports is not limited to physical training, but especially in mental training. Every athlete, in terms of private morals, should pay attention to physical and mental cleanliness, and eliminate all bad habits. In terms of public morals, all actions should be collective and disciplined; otherwise, being scattered and disorganized will inevitably lead to courage in private fights but cowardice in public battles. With twelve points of courage and perseverance, take on the responsibility of transforming weakness into strength. May your moral character be as clean as water, your patriotism be as fierce as fire, and your spirit and body be as strong as steel."

Alas, the world is changing rapidly, and the nation is facing imminent destruction. The responsibility for revitalization and self-strengthening falls on no one else. Athletes, the nation's elite, should remember the profound farewell words of the national education officials, recognize the precarious situation of the Chinese nation, deeply understand the significance of this sports meet in strengthening the race and revitalizing the country, take on the responsibility of restoring China and defending the country, strive forward and act vigorously, do not indulge in playing with things and lose your ambition, work hard and practice diligently, be afraid of private fights and be brave in public battles, do not be calculating about the victory or defeat of individuals, or be concerned about the shortness of the day, you should diligently seek the health of your own body and mind in order to forge your courage and ability to produce and fight for the nation. Then the outcome of this conference will not be an extravagant display of success or a meaningless waste, but will have a different and great value. October 1933, in Shanghai.

Page 15

Spring and Autumn

Officialdom 233

— Shi Xian

"Raising the right hand, swearing to take office," and "Resigning repeatedly, telegraphing resignation" -- these two things, except for those who do not read newspapers, or who read newspapers but only look at "Today's Great Light Reflects the All-Powerful Woman," or "Mei Lanfang Will Take the Stage Soon" friends, generally feel that this is "rise and fall in officialdom" common meal, and nothing more.

But if we close our eyes and think about it, then, in this common meal of "rise and fall in officialdom," there are many incredible flavors.

In every letter of resignation, there are always sentences that bring tears to the eyes, such as "exhausted from overwork" and "mentally and physically exhausted." Even "repeatedly resigning" fully expresses the pain of "not being allowed to get rid of the official hat." It can be seen that being an official is not as enjoyable as we ordinary people who have never been officials imagine. And those who want to get rid of the official hat resign once, twice, and even three times, being held back by the arm and not allowed to throw it away. It is said that this is because there is no suitable successor, and there is a sense that "if this gentleman leaves, what will happen to the people?" Therefore, officials who understand "enduring hardship and resentment," although they suffer, are not easy to resign.

But if an official who "endures hardship and resentment" really "becomes ill from overwork" and "mentally and physically exhausted" and resigns again and again, then who will be willing to take over is another great problem. Although on the one hand, "the resignation is just approved," on the other hand, someone has already been "appointed" to a certain position, but as soon as someone raises their right hand and swears to take office, there must immediately be a telegram of "firm refusal is not accepted, reluctantly taking on difficult tasks" to express one hundred and twenty thousand points of grievance, and it is not that they love to put the official hat on their heads.

Therefore, we really cannot regard the rise and fall between "a new official taking office and an old official leaving" as a trivial matter, but should realize that this is another batch jumping into the fire pit.

From the above, we can see the boredom of "officialdom," so only a non-fool should be an official. Even "three visits to the thatched cottage, and firm refusal is not accepted," at most, one can only "reluctantly take on difficult tasks, waiting for the capable," and as soon as there is an opportunity, one should withdraw cleanly to give way to the capable. Ji Hongchang and Fang Zhenwu were utterly defeated, but still asked for "name" and "military commander," really fools. There are also some unnamed alternate officials who are always waving eight-line letters and running around to curry favor with the powerful, desperately wanting to float and sink in officialdom, which is even more foolish to the extreme.

Pirated Books 234

— Yan Qiao

A few years ago, piracy was not a problem. You could print "All rights reserved, reproduction will be prosecuted," and people would turn a blind eye. Recently, the publishing industry in Shanghai has refused to give up and is gradually paying attention to this. Once discovered, they would negotiate, and if reconciliation fails, they would seek legal remedies. If the piracy is in a remote place, they can only open their eyes wide and wring their hands without a solution.

Now some clever people do not pirate Chinese books, but pirate foreign books. It may be said that the Chinese publishing industry has not joined the International Copyright Alliance, and can legally evade responsibility, and there is only something that cannot be said morally. In fact, this is a high-sounding statement. The magic lies in the fact that the original publisher is tens of thousands of miles away, so-called out of reach.

However, due to the exorbitant price of gold and the meager purchasing power of students, they must be allowed to choose convenient purchases. Therefore, two interesting things happened in our Suzhou:

One is that the foreign principal of School A absolutely forbids students from buying pirated foreign books in order to maintain his foreign morality. And the Chinese principal of School B said to the foreign teacher, "We Chinese have more important rights than books that have been invaded by foreigners." Therefore, School B allows students to do as they please.

One is that the ethics professor of School C is a foreigner and asked the students, "Are you willing to buy pirated books?" Because this question is related to ethics itself, it is difficult for the students to answer, so they have to remain silent. The foreign professor then asked, "How much is the price difference between the original and the pirated version?" One student answered, "The original version requires more than fourteen yuan, and the pirated version does not cost more than four yuan." The foreign professor smiled and then remained silent.

Recently, an American chemist said in the preface to the reprinted edition of his chemistry textbook: "I am very happy to see a Chinese pirated book." This chemist has a lot of humor.

What Does it Mean 235

— Dao An

People's age, of course, increases year by year, but the age of modern women not only does not increase, but also greatly reverses. For example, she was twenty-four years old last year, but this year, she only says she is twenty-two years old. Next year, she may even regress to eighteen or nineteen years old. What does this mean?

The number of times that modern women use mirrors to look at their faces, calculated on average per day, is probably more than a hundred times, right? From getting up, washing their faces, putting on makeup, drawing eyebrows, applying powder, applying rouge, putting on lipstick, putting on clothes, putting on shoes, or when going out, in addition to horizontal and vertical reflections, they also look in the mirror when walking and sitting in the car. When watching plays and movies, they always take special photos. If someone gives her a Liu Zhen stare, her mirror work becomes even busier. What does this mean?

Women have the right for two or three people to sit in a rickshaw, while men can only sigh at the sight of the car and cannot enjoy this right. What does this mean?

The filial sons of the bereaved family mostly line a piece of red cloth on the heels of the hemp shoes they wear during the initial mourning period. What does this mean?

People who mess around in the sea of love mostly end up disappointed in love (except for the rich). There are few who are successful in love. What does this mean?

Not Valuing Sons, Valuing Daughters 236

— Yi Yi Guan Zhu

For thousands of years, we Chinese have had a tradition and concept, that is, "valuing sons and belittling daughters." It is said that "daughters are money-losing goods." When a daughter is born, she is raised with great difficulty, and then given away to someone else. People feel that it is not easy. Look, those who choose a son-in-law for their daughters, poor households certainly do not want a son-in-law who is not a rich man, and rich families dislike the official not being handsome. Even if our old man likes what he sees, he does not know what our daughter thinks. This is wrong, that is not a match, how much trouble! Although it is said that everyone now emphasizes freedom, this fee for a free son-in-law is enough for you to bear. The first is to send them to school to study, and the second is to dress them up like flowers, so that someone will pursue them, so that they can be free and fall in love. When they fall in love and succeed, you need not worry about how little dowry there is that the father can bear. Otherwise, you will be looked down upon, and your daughter will have a hard time in the world. As for saying that the son-in-law is half a son to depend on, this is a joke and a strange tale. You must know that the son-in-law, Mr. Official, is somewhat polite, no matter how you depend on him; only your son can handle the funeral when you are old. Is it possible to call the son-in-law to hold the head and claim to be an orphan? Alas! For thousands of years, we Chinese have had the concept of "valuing sons and belittling daughters," perhaps for all the reasons mentioned above?

However, since ancient times, there have been many who have relied on their daughters to enjoy wealth and glory. As long as your daughter is as beautiful as an angel, and can win people's praise as an "angel," that is your good fortune and endless hope. At the very least, she does not need you to worry when she goes out alone. Naturally, there are many volunteer bodyguards who follow her around, and if she encounters a stray dog, it will definitely not bite her thigh. As for the question of choosing a son-in-law, naturally, you do not need to worry at all. Not to mention foreign firms and bank executives wanting to become related, even the rich people have to ask matchmakers to say that the marriage is reasonable. At that time, the mother-in-law looks at the son-in-law, and the more she looks, the more interesting he becomes. Is there still the idea of "valuing sons and belittling daughters"?

Alas! Originally, in this world, saying "valuing sons and belittling daughters" is really the number one fool. You must know that "not valuing sons but valuing daughters" is the only hope.

Brief News: The People's Artist Juezhu. Since his unique style of one-yuan store Kunjiagu engraving came out, there have been many seekers. Recently, he has expressed his weariness of the news business and is devoting himself to writing a small dictionary of Jiagu and records of different characters from previous dynasties. Those who seek his works, please contact Du Yu at No. 10 Yuqing Lane, Gordon Road. Please attach postage to the letter requesting the fee, and it will be sent immediately.

The Rise and Fall of the World is Everyone's Responsibility 237

— Pin Shan

Some people say: "Mr. Gu Yanwu's famous saying: "The rise and fall of the world is everyone's responsibility." The word "responsibility" should be changed to "debt." Look, in today's country, internal and external debts are stacked on top of each other, and old debts have not been cleared, and new debts are coming. All of these debts, in the end, are borne by our ordinary people. Isn't this called: "The rise and fall of the world is everyone's debt?""

Four Northeast Company Commanders 238

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter 18: Silently Passing Tea to Comfort Her Husband, Hurriedly Leaving the Border, Forcing a Smile to Say Goodbye to Her Family

Old Zhao knew that the sigh contained a great deal of unsaid words. But if he really spoke them out, his son would probably be unable to bear it. Because in the past two days, he had heard a lot of idle talk from Mrs. Jiang. The meaning was always that the girl was originally afraid of marrying a soldier, because soldiers are not easy to be at home often. Now that they are just engaged, the son-in-law is about to leave, and this matter will be difficult to say in the future. This time, Old Zhao did not wait for him to say the words, and immediately grabbed the words and said: There are long-distance buses from Xifengkou to Beijing, and you can come back in more than a day. In the future, when we have a happy event, we are willing to go to Xifengkou to hold it there. If we are not willing to go to Xifengkou, Ziqiang can come back when the day comes, it's not a big deal. Zhao Ziqiang said: That's right, it's very convenient to come and go. Mrs. Jiang was silent for five minutes, and then said: When the son-in-law leaves, he will be promoted and make money, this is a good thing. Naturally, he will win every battle and achieve success immediately, what else can I say? It would be good if we could do it according to the son-in-law's way of doing things. Zhao Ziqiang felt that these words were getting closer and closer to complaining, so he changed the subject and said: Dad, I also thought of one thing. Company Commander Tian said that he had already called Miss Huang Manying twice, asking him to come to Haidian, but he could not leave to go to the city. According to my meaning, if Miss Huang comes, please ask him to rest here for one night. We will leave tomorrow, anyway, we will pass through Haidian Street, so we will meet. It is best to ask you to hire someone to go to the city and ask him to leave the city immediately. Then, when I return to the camp, I can ask Company Commander Tian to come here once. Mrs. Jiang smiled faintly and said: You have this time to take care of other people's business. Although this was a joke, Zhao Ziqiang felt that these words were twenty-four points serious, so he smiled and said: Last night, the departure time has not been determined yet, Company Commander Tian was saying this, today I am back, I naturally want to think about this matter. Personal Small Record

Interview with Liang Tongfang 239

— Qi Yu

After the fall of the Northeast, those with a bit of spirit in the country were extremely indignant. I think everyone feels the same way except for the non-resistance general. But as time passed, the call for resistance gradually weakened. Opening the newspaper, the words "resistance against Japan" gradually decreased. The names and whereabouts of general anti-Japanese comrades are not easy to see. Not long ago, there was an anti-Japanese major general, Jiang Minsheng, who ended up in Shanghai, shining shoes for people. Recently, there has been an anti-Japanese comrade, Liang Tongfang, pulling a rickshaw. The result of resisting Japan is like this, while those who do not resist Japan are living a life of enjoyment, spending their days drinking and having fun. Compared, it is really both ridiculous and sad. Since the news of Liang Tongfang was spread in various newspapers, I have been a friend of Lawyer Yao Zhaoli, and Liang often appears at the door of Lawyer Yao, so I especially asked Lawyer Yao to make an appointment with Liang yesterday afternoon. At about five o'clock, I met with Liang at Lawyer Yao's office. Liang has a fair complexion and is of medium height. He is wearing a khaki Zhongshan suit and is very kind. He is from Yu Ren, Zhejiang. He has done business in money houses. When the January 28th Incident occurred, he joined the Shanghai Citizens' Volunteer Army. Later, he served as a student in General Weng Zhaoyuan's unit. After the term expired, he joined the Shanghai Student Army Northeast Volunteer Group and went to the front line to fight. At that time, he wanted to go straight to Huanglong, but who knew that the result would be like this. After coming to Shanghai, because it was not easy to find a suitable job for a while, he decided to pull a rickshaw to support himself and was unwilling to accept any financial assistance from relatives and friends. He had been in Shanghai for several days, because he was an amateur in renting a rickshaw and did not know the procedure. After running for five or six days, there was still no result. Fortunately, Lawyer Yao's cousin, Ms. Ruifang, had an introduction letter for him to see Yao when she came south. At that time, Lawyer Yao's intention was to provide him with economic assistance, but Liang resolutely declined, saying that pulling a rickshaw was not a bad profession. In the end, Lawyer Yao had to find a way to rent a rickshaw for him, with a daily rent of six jiao and five fen of silver dollars.

When I met Liang, he had only been pulling a rickshaw for the fourth day. It is said that once he pulled a guest who said he wanted to go to a certain place in the French Concession, but suddenly asked him to pull him to the door of a restaurant outside the New North Gate. After the man jumped out of the car, he looked at Liang carefully and suddenly asked Liang if he was the Liang mentioned in the newspaper who was an anti-Japanese comrade. Liang initially did not answer, but after he insisted on asking, he had to say yes. The man was very happy and insisted on inviting him in to eat together. Liang refused, but was eventually picked up by him and brought in. It is said that this man's surname is Tu and he runs a cotton wool factory on Longhua Road. After reading the newspaper, he expressed great sympathy for Liang. There is also a Feixing Car Company, which sent several bicycles to search for the rickshaw with his information in order to find Liang. In the end, they found it and invited him to talk for half a day. Reporters from other newspapers and news agencies went to Lawyer Yao's office to interview him in an endless stream.

I asked Liang how his whereabouts became known to newspaper reporters. Liang said: I have been in Shanghai for many days. I want to pull a rickshaw because I want to use it as a temporary profession. As soon as there is an anti-Japanese opportunity, I still want to go out. I don't want to use this to show off, but that day I was at Lawyer Yao's place, and a reporter from Fuxing News Agency happened to be here. So Lawyer Yao introduced him and the reporter talked. The next day, many newspapers published the news.

Finally, Liang said: I am very lucky to be able to return to Shanghai. There are still seven comrades who went with me who are still in the snow and ice. Because they have no financial assistance, they are very distressed and cannot return. Now that resisting Japan has become a thing of the past, I sincerely hope that all circles in Shanghai can find a way to rescue them. The names of the seven comrades are Zhang Muren, Zhu Xueming, Huang Xiegen, Yu Gengsheng, Ni Huaixin, Jin Zhong, and Zou Tianxi. After Liang finished speaking, he couldn't help but sigh. Coincidentally, another newspaper reporter came to visit, so I took my leave.

At this time, the lights of thousands of homes had long been lit, and the music in the dance hall was ringing. Champagne...inside...happy...a drunken soul will never know the pain of a country's destruction!

Grains, Futures, Flour, Wheat Surge and Retreat Sharply, Morning Rumors of Tax on Foreign Wheat, Afternoon Confirmation that Foreign Wheat Would Be Agreed Upon 254

In the flour market yesterday morning, there were rumors of a tax on foreign wheat. Market sentiment was agitated and buyers did their best to purchase, causing a sharp rise, which was rarely seen before. Prices for all months rose sharply, with the current month rising by as much as $2.2, and the forward months even more so, with prices exceeding the previous day's closing price by 50-60 cents. In the afternoon, it was confirmed that this tax was not to be fully believed, and the major factories did their best to sell, short sellers increased their positions, and long sellers returned, causing an even more dramatic decline. Prices suddenly fell by a significant amount of about one dollar in five rounds. The closing price saw a decline, with the closing price for December being down by 3.5 cents, the current month down by 2.25 cents, February down by 3 cents, March down by 2.5 cents, and April down by 2 cents.

The wheat market yesterday saw dramatic changes, with a sharp rise in the morning and a dramatic decline in the afternoon, with fluctuations of over one dollar during the day. The market rose sharply in the morning due to rumors that a tax on foreign wheat would be implemented, with January rising by 1.8 cents and other months rising by 1.6-1 cent. In the afternoon, it was confirmed that foreign wheat prices had fallen, and the government had agreed to lend 15,000 tons of US wheat at a price of only $4.15, and it was rumored that a total of 25,000 tons were involved. As a result, various parties competed to sell, and prices immediately fell by over one dollar. The closing price for the current month remained the same as the previous day, the next month was up by 3 cents, and the remaining months were up by 5 cents.

Generally, because western Hubei is far from Wuhan, and transportation by waterway is subject to delays during the dry season of the Yangtze River's upper reaches in winter, it is unavoidable. Only Macheng oil can be transported by road, but it is feared that it will not arrive in Wuhan until after the Major Snow solar term. Therefore, every year when the new oil in Zhejiang Province is already in full swing, Wuhan is still selling old inventory. Thus, during the transition between old and new inventory, the situation in Wuhan and Shanghai is slightly different. Currently, new goods have been sampled in Zhejiang's eastern areas such as Jinlan. According to the letter from Lanxi a few days ago, merchants have received dozens of pieces of new oil, with a purchase price of 16 yuan per piece. Although the price of the new oil is not yet accurate, the overall trend suggests it will not deviate far. Although western Zhejiang has not reported on the new harvest, it will be within half a month. Shanghai, being close to Zhejiang Province, naturally does not pay much attention to the old oil in Wuhan. Therefore, although the price of Macheng oil in Wuhan has increased from 17 yuan and 7 or 8 cents to 18 yuan and 2 or 3 cents, merchants in Shanghai are not very excited, as their attention is focused on the new goods from Zhejiang Province. However, the price fluctuations in Wuhan affect the overall situation. The Zhejiang province is seeing more brisk sales of old inventories, but it is hoped that the prices will drop too low, making it difficult to approach for the time being, so transactions have not yet been made. It is expected that transactions of new goods will be discovered within ten days. In recent days, the sales price of old oil has not changed. Jingzhou double-layered oil is priced at 22 yuan and slightly more, Pingjing at 21 yuan and 5 or 6 cents, and Suocheng oil at slightly below 20 yuan.

Informal Essays

Beauty and Choosing a Wife 264

— Guanghan

After reading Mr. Binfu's "Money and Choosing a Husband" in this publication, I was inspired to write this article ("Beauty and Choosing a Wife," 1) to serve as a counterpart.

Regarding the selection of a husband or wife, many have always ridiculed women for making "money" the main condition for choosing a husband. This is indeed the case, and it is a psychological mistake on the part of women. Little do they know that men, when choosing a wife, also fall into a kind of prejudice, often taking "beauty" as the standard for an "ideal wife."

Understanding the reason why women value "money," there is no doubt that this is because women mostly have a kind of "vanity." To satisfy this vanity, they cannot help but rely on the power of money to achieve their goals. Therefore, their "ideal husband" must be a man with abundant financial resources. As for men choosing women based on "beauty," what is the intention behind this? To say it bluntly, it is nothing more than satisfying their "sexual desire" (in a broad sense). Because a beautiful wife naturally provides her husband with more satisfactory sexual comfort than an ugly wife. Therefore, those seeking a partner all hope to find an angelic companion.

This is where the problem arises. Aren't we saying that women's emphasis on "money" is wrong? Hasn't this mistake been condemned by countless people? What about men's emphasis on "beauty"? Could this be a proper psychology? If not, why is it that so few people have noticed this point, and we have never heard any attacks? What is the reason for this? There is no other reason than that the world is still a male-centered world, so men always have the advantage, and women always suffer.

When it comes to choosing a partner, it naturally varies from person to person, and there is no fixed standard. Some value this, and some value that. It is naturally impossible for you to point out who is reasonable and who is unreasonable. However, we must understand that if a man and a woman want to live together in both good times and bad, then both sides' character, knowledge, thoughts, habits, behaviors, and health are all very important and should be taken care of. Money and beauty can only be regarded as one of the many conditions and cannot be used as the main goal of choice. Therefore, women's emphasis on "money" is wrong, and men's emphasis on "beauty" is also wrong. Can we only blame women and forgive men?

The above refers to a proper marriage between a man and a woman. As for some "materialistic" women and "sex-obsessed" men, that's another matter. Because they only know how to satisfy "material desires" and "sexual desires," and everything else is irrelevant. In this situation, women only value "money," and men only value "beauty." Women who have "money" can sacrifice anything, and men who have "beauty" can give up everything. This is very unreasonable. How many men and women in society have been led to destruction by these needs? This is a very painful thing. Therefore, I believe that "vanity" is indeed a woman's weakness, and "beauty worship" is precisely a man's lack of virtue!

Game Writing

Grandma Sutra 265

— Shen Min

I am now going to recite the Grandma Sutra, virtuous men and faithful women, listen carefully,

Whoever recites my Grandma Sutra, the whole family, old and young, will be at peace,

If no one recites my Grandma Sutra, the family will be turned upside down, and there will be no peace,

Although Grandma was humble when she was young, she is now blessed with good fortune,

Grandma is still young, this year she is eighteen years old,

Naturally beautiful, her face is like a flower, the most modern of 1933,

The beautiful scenery of spring mountains is like a painting, the amorous feelings in her eyes are like autumn water,

Unique peaks add to the spring scenery, fleshy and plump add to the charm,

All living beings are captivated under her cheongsam, she is a social butterfly in the social scene,

She dances and plays mahjong at night, and sleeps until three o'clock in the daytime,

The Western-style building is really comfortable, and a motorcycle is used for transportation,

Maids and servants are at her beck and call, and there is a large group of maids and nannies,

The young master obeys her in everything, being docile and gentle,

When I am about to get up, he helps me tidy my clothes,

He helps me put on my high-heeled leather shoes, and even puts powder on my face,

He brings delicious food to my mouth when I eat porridge, rice, and snacks,

If we go out to play, we walk side by side, arm in arm,

People say we are blessed with romance, and everyone is enchanted when they see us,

We swagger through the streets, full of vigor, whispering sweet nothings,

The other day, a blind fortune-teller came to tell my fortune, saying that I am going to have good luck,

When the aviation lottery is drawn, I will have a share of 500,000 gold coins,

Regardless of yellow disasters and black disasters, burning incense and worshiping Buddha are the right things to do,

What loving the country or not loving the country, I wear imported clothing,

I am completely Westernized, full of foreign airs, and I do not ask about the national crisis,

I don't care about anything, and I sincerely recite the Grandma Sutra,

Escape 266

— Wenbing

Recently, something strange has happened at the second landlord's house. The most obvious thing is that the decorations in the luxurious living room have all been moved to the second young lady's bedroom on the third floor. At the same time, a "Living Room for Rent" sign was posted on the front door. As a result, the mahjong game that used to be noisy all day long, even the one that was often opened in the second young lady's bedroom, has all fallen silent.

Secondly, one day at around noon, in the second young lady's bedroom, the wife was present, and the young lady's husband was also present. At first, they mumbled something indistinctly, then all three fell silent. After a while, the young lady began to cry, and the husband propped his cheeks with both hands, lowered his head dejectedly. As for the wife, she stood there like a wooden chicken, staring blankly.

Thirdly, the wife is always in a panic every day, like a shuttle weaving back and forth on the "zigzag" shaped staircase, climbing from the living room to the third floor, and then climbing down to the kitchen. Moreover, when she passed my room, she was no longer the grim-faced person she used to be, but her face was full of bitter smiles, and she greeted me for no reason. Sometimes, when she saw my socks that had been knocked off the chair and onto the ground by my back, she would immediately enter the room and pick them up for me, saying, "Mr. Kuang, you really work hard, your socks fell on the ground!"

In addition, the second young lady, who used to be so proud and aloof, has also become exceptionally humble. When she passed by on the staircase, she always gave me a flirtatious glance, which made me suspect that she had gone crazy, making my heart flutter strangely. Sometimes, I even wanted to "make a move" on her.

In addition, the wife also had a robust eldest daughter, who lived in the shed on the drying terrace with a group of dirty children. According to the wife, the eldest daughter's life was miserable enough, and her husband's family simply had no food to eat. Therefore, she had no choice but to come here to beg for food. A few days ago, after a big fight, she was driven away by the second young lady.

This situation has lasted for a week, and it is like a mystery to me. I can't figure it out no matter what, and I don't feel comfortable asking. Moreover, I am a guest from out of town, and I have always been lonely. I have never had any contact with the front building, the back building, or the neighbors on the left and right. Suddenly, I don't feel comfortable discussing this sudden strangeness of the second landlord with them.

A mystery is, after all, a mystery.

However, I am confident that this mystery probably has nothing to do with me!

It was late at night, and I was reading Lu Xun's "A Call to Arms," specifically the story of Kong Yiji. When I read the part where Kong Yiji stared at the few remaining fennel beans, shook his head, and recited to the children, "Not much, not much, is it much? Not much." I was laughing so hard that tears were streaming from my eyes. There was a series of urgent knocks on the door outside, followed by the wife entering. The second young lady also twisted her body and appeared in front of my desk. Their exceptional politeness made me feel fearful and uneasy.

"Mr. Kuang, I'm very sorry, I want to discuss something with you..." the wife said, then stopped.

"Sure, what is it?" I readily agreed with her. The second young lady smiled sweetly at the side (obviously a bitter smile). Only then did the wife continue, as if choking:

"Mr. Kuang, you know, our 老閭 (boss, here referring to husband) works on a ship, and he earns quite a bit. But he is getting old and still acting like a fool, throwing money into the pockets of a mistress in Hankou, completely disregarding his own family. The second daughter's husband has also been having difficulties recently, which has resulted in arrears of more than nine months of rent to the big landlord, more than 500 taels. It's really impossible to think about. We have no choice but to temporarily avoid this. We want to deposit a few valuable pieces of furniture in Mr. Kuang's room to avoid being sealed off. We will find a way to take them away in a few days!"

I repeatedly said, "It's originally possible, but..." The nanny outside the door rolled the boxes and cabinets in. The second young lady even said she wanted to move in her brass bed, which cost eighty silver dollars. I was so anxious that I blocked the door, and that was how I stopped her.

That's how my small building became their vault. Seeing how pitiful they were, I really didn't know what to do at the time, and I didn't dare to push them out of the room right away. I just wanted to talk to them in detail tomorrow and think of another way. The landlord's wife was so flustered that she couldn't speak clearly, and just said intermittently: "Please...help...please! The big landlord is coming to check, say it's yours."

When I woke up the next day, I really didn't expect that they had all escaped early in the morning, maybe they had escaped last night.

As a result, the neighborhood has been in a state of commotion until now.

Ying 267

— Ren

Ying is sick, so sick that she doesn't look like a person! Today, I heard the doctor say that she is suffering from consumption. Alas, consumption is a "money disease"! Is Ying, who has no money, worthy of suffering from this disease? She is lying there waiting to die!

Ying, as I look at Ying lying on the deck chair, thin and yellow like dried firewood, she is not yet thirty years old, but her youth has long withered away! No, in her short life, there is no such thing as youth. All she has are heartbreaking and sad memories.

At the age of eighteen, by the order of her parents and the words of a matchmaker, she married Mei Jun. In the first year or two of their marriage, they were still able to live peacefully. But in the last five years, the situation has changed greatly. Mei Jun, a person with no skills who only relied on smooth talk to make a living, should of course be swayed by the waves of the times and become unemployed. However, she, who toiled like a horse and an ox at home all day long, was not only abused by her parents-in-law and given the cold shoulder by her sisters-in-law, but was also unconditionally driven out of the family. The reason was that Ying's fate was too bad, causing her husband to be disabled at home and unable to do business. Although Mei Jun was their only beloved son, and Ying was their beloved daughter-in-law, in the old people who were deeply entrenched in patriarchal concepts, adhering to the ancestral teachings of "raising sons to guard against old age," there was nothing strange about their love for their son and daughter-in-law, who could not bring money to show their filial piety, dropping from a boiling point to a freezing point.

Five years ago, Mei Jun was still an employee at XX Company, and his monthly income was not bad. But "sated with food and warm clothes, one thinks of lust." How could a monthly salary of over a hundred yuan be enough for him to squander at will? For a whole week, or even a whole month, he would not return home, causing Ying to strain her eyes waiting, stretching her neck in vain anticipation. Sometimes, she could not close her eyes all night. On cool nights, she had to sleep alone under the quilt, secretly weeping bitterly to endure the long night. When Mei Jun came home, she still ignored her, but she had to flatter him, because in the psychology of old-fashioned women, they thought that their husband was the only sacred "backbone," so how could they not be diligent towards him? Even a moment of carelessness in speech would result in his punches and kicks, which was very common.

Mei Jun was eventually dismissed by the company's boss for being too promiscuous. Thus, his economic lifeline was undoubtedly cut off. How could he restrain himself from his accustomed extravagance? His eyes also became blind due to his previous excessive indulgence. Thus, he could not move anything and could only sit and wait for death to come. But the god of death was strangely forgiving of him and did not come to catch him. His stomach could not be tied tight, and he still had to eat when he was hungry. Poor Ying, a thin and frail woman like dried firewood, had suffered enough uncompensated torture in her life. At this time, she was implicated in her own fate due to her husband's incompetence and was driven out!

She is sick, so sick that she doesn't look like a person! In a small room the size of a斗 (dou, unit of volume), I look at her disheveled hair, her thin yellow face, her sunken eyes, and her withered hands, and I see a hideous black shadow flashing in this small house.

Writings and Casual Conversation 268

— Yazhu

The great British philosopher Herbert Spencer only associated with close friends throughout his life, and he would never meet strangers. The reason:

"A person's brilliance 丨丨 the best products produced by the mind, are all in his writings. Only the dregs remain by his side for everyday conversation."

Because a brilliant theory, if explained simply, will not be understood and often leads to misunderstanding or misinterpretation. If explained in detail (usually friends do not gather to lecture and debate as in a school), people find it annoying, impatient, and unwilling to listen to the end. Before you can finish explaining, others may interrupt or take things out of context to argue, or even sneer, making you very angry and upset. Even with close friends, one must be cautious. Therefore, brilliant theories must be written down. The material for writing and conversation must be completely separated:

The brilliant is committed to writing.

The non-brilliant is used for conversation.

The more brilliant the writing, the better.

The more casual the conversation, the better.

In general, young people with more thoughts initially entering the world feel that chatting with others is extremely meaningless. Because they are not allowed to converse with people, or if they do converse, they must talk about important events or theories, thinking that is more meaningful. Unexpectedly, after only saying a word or two, they are misunderstood or annoyed, often unable to clarify, and they are not allowed to explain their true feelings, doing more harm than good, and they are infuriated. Because there is a barrier between people. The more worldly a person is, the more suspicious he is, and they are all very subjective. As soon as you talk about a theory, he does not first care whether your theory is right or wrong, but first guesses the background of your discussion, or suspects that you are flaunting your intelligence, or suspects that you are secretly talking about him. He will then disagree with you. This is also impossible to explain, because he thinks that if it is not about him, why should he start a discussion with him? If they are too young, they cannot discuss anything with you. If they are more knowledgeable and older than you, they want to maintain their dignity, adhere to their own views, and harbor the prejudice that young people cannot have high opinions, leaving no room for discussion. Unless they are close friends, one must be careful even with ordinary casual conversation.

Initially, the purpose of writing was not to express opinions but to gain literary fame. Then, they feel that brilliant theories cannot be talked about with people, and the scope of oral transmission is very narrow, so they must write and publish. At this time, the desire for fame has diminished, and they focus on gaining sympathy for their theories. However, having a name makes it easier for people to believe or value their opinions.

Finally, as their theories become increasingly refined, they cannot be talked about with the few people they are close to. These brilliant products of the mind should not be enjoyed alone, and they can promote the development of the world, so they are unwilling to let them disappear. Like a woman who is pregnant, carrying a fetus for ten months, they cannot help but give birth. Because they cannot avoid engaging in writing and publishing it to the world. At this time, they only have a sense of responsibility and no desire for fame.

Modern celebrity calligraphy and painting, Mr. Hanying Landscape Painting

Deviant Economic Independence 269

— Xin

1. I attended a banquet held in X 前 a couple days ago. A woman who appeared to be a mannish figure came to our student team in the banquet room. After being introduced by a guest, I also talked to her. I don’t know why, but we needed to ask her to write her address. She said, “I can’t write it.” At first, we thought she was being polite. Later, we found out that she really didn’t know how to write. At the time, we were surprised to learn that she was illiterate, but also a very modern lady with short hair. After she left, a group of students who were eager to find out about everything heard the following from another female guest, “She is 24 years old this year, and she divorced her husband two years ago. Because she didn’t have the ability to support herself, she joined the dance hall and became a variant of economic independence. She is currently wandering at a crossroads between a dancehall and acting. She is an unofficial dancer and celebrity.”

Ah! Women can be found everywhere now! This is something to celebrate. After the women's rights movement was popular for a while, we see that it has achieved some success. But in general, there are always things to regret. The word “flower vase” is an attractive noun awarded to company clerks whose monthly allowance is just enough to buy make-up. Their economic independence is great, but people say they engage in some kind of business.

Dance halls were established for people’s entertainment and places for women to sell their bodies with their touching meat and graceful attire. Who can deny that? Let’s talk about the latest trend of movies that most people recognize as an educational tool. Given that it is highly regarded by everyone, the movie industry has a big responsibility to educate the public. If an illiterate woman, like the female guest mentioned earlier, were to act in a movie, what practical education could they get from these actors? Other than their charming, alluring eyes, crimson lips, big breasts, and fleshy thighs… other than the sensual and seductive ways to enchant their audience, we can’t talk about any kind of artistic meaning. People are either thoughtlessly cheering or want to promote their products, so they take advantage of the actresses and make extravagant ads. Ah! They should be more conscious. Although they can earn a lot of money every day, they become parasites and the cause of the current chaos and unrest! At best, it is a variant of economic independence, because we should understand the important responsibilities we have. We should be using our talents to earn the appropriate amount of payment.

On a Public Bus 270

— Person

Basket took the No. 9 public bus to Avenue Foch. On such a long journey, I sat with someone with nothing to do, so I took out a book and started reading it intentionally or unintentionally. A large group of passengers got on, and a large group got off. I didn't notice anything until a foreign ticket inspector came to check my ticket. Then I realized it was the ticket inspector. A strange drama thus began:

On the side of the bus where the driver was, on one of the seats, sat a middle-aged man, holding some kind of bottle in his hand. All the other passengers on the bus had already bought their tickets. Only he was still clutching the coins tightly in his palm. When the ticket inspector came to check his ticket, he asked, "How much is it to XX Road?" The foreign ticket inspector took the coins, smiled sarcastically, went to the ticket seller to exchange for a ticket, and then handed it to him. He then wrote something silently in a notebook, without saying a word. (Because he was considered to be trying to "mooch" from the ticket buyer). Silently standing in the bus, listening to the ticket seller and the man with the bottle arguing. "You troublemaker, sitting silently in the corner. You son of a bitch, trying to mooch, causing others to be fined, you shameless thing," the ticket seller cursed fiercely.

"You are a shameless little dog thing, trying to mooch yourself, why don't you just sell tickets, and still scold others, be careful!" The other party also turned pale and retorted defiantly, holding on to his self-righteous grounds.

"Careful of what? Sitting here silently like a ghost, why did everyone else buy a ticket except you?"

"It's obvious you want to mooch!"

"I really don't want to mooch, the money from mooching will be used for scraping therapy. A shameless troublemaker like you should by rights have to pay the full thirty-four cents, who knows where you crawled out from..."

"..."

The foreign ticket inspector stood there quietly, as if understanding or not, his two eyeballs hidden in the yellow hair, shining brightly as he gazed at them. A thin gentleman sitting next to me, wearing a black long gown and a tilted felt hat, opened his mouth to comment: "We are not in the know, but you two yourselves know what's going on in your hearts. But you are mooching from the foreigners, why are you arguing so seriously? We are all Chinese, making fools of ourselves in front of foreigners because of the foreigners' affairs, how embarrassing is that!" (To the ticket seller:) "Can't you tell the difference? Why do you start cursing people as soon as you open your mouth? That's not right of you!"...

The destination arrived. The thin gentleman's strange argument had not yet reached a conclusion. I had no choice but to jump off the bus, regretting that I didn't have the good fortune to hear the end, and took a deep breath.

Drama

War and Peace (60) (A Four-Act Play) 271

— Dai He

Act Four: Where to Go? Scene Two

Soldier C: Everyone, don't panic, stay calm. Every bullet we fire must kill one of them.

Soldier G: No, I'm not fighting anymore, I want to go back.

(He crawls outwards. Soldier B pulls him back.)

Soldier B: Are you crazy? With so many bullets, you want to go and die?

Soldier G: No, don't hold me back, let me out.

(Two soldiers are hit and fall to the ground. Soldier G is also hit and falls from the trench.)

Soldier G: Ouch, my mother! ... Ouch!

Soldier A: That's what he deserves! We told him not to crawl out, but he had to crawl out like a child.

Soldier G: Ouch, ouch...

Soldier D: Where is he hit? Quickly get a cloth to tie it up.

Soldier B: Right in the stomach.

Soldier G: Heaven, my mother! ...

Soldier D: Hey, give him another shot, it's useless anyway, why make him suffer!

Soldier B: I won't do it.

Soldier A: What's the matter, are you afraid?

Soldier E: If you shoot him, you'll be doing him a favor.

Soldier B: I dare not, my gun doesn't shoot my own people.

Soldier A: You useless fellow, wait for me.

Soldier D: Aim at his head!

Soldier A: I'll send you back home!

(Soldier A shoots. Soldier G stops moving. Everyone is horrified.)

Soldier H: If you have to die, you should die quickly, like this, not dying with one shot and needing another, it's really too painful.

Soldier B: Why are you shouting injustice, hurry up and shoot!

(Suddenly the enemy gunfire stops,) only the sound of intense running.)

Soldier D: Huh? What's going on? Why aren't the enemy firing anymore?

Soldier A: Hmph, we have to be careful now, they're going to charge over again. (Sound of tanks)

Soldier E: Listen, the tanks are coming too.

Soldier C: Brothers, let's get our hand grenades ready.

Soldier B: But we don't have many hand grenades left.

Soldier A: What are you afraid of if we don't have hand grenades? We have broadswords and bayonets, we have hot blood and heads. Come on, brothers, pick up our broadswords, fix our bayonets, and wait!

(Enemy shells land in the battlefield, smoke fills the air, dust flies everywhere. Our army sets up machine guns, fixes bayonets, and waits in full battle array. Lightning flashes, illuminating the extremely tense faces of everyone. Afterwards, the sound of a charge is faintly heard in the distance. Shouts of killing from far to near. The sound of cutting barbed wire nearby.)

Film Special

The Secrets to Finding Work in Hollywood (Part 1) 272

— Guang Dao

Kim Harlow's Experience: The First Key is Patience

You often see unknown names suddenly enter the Hollywood film industry and become famous overnight. Of course, you are very envious. But you can't find a way in; every time you write to those stars or film companies, asking them how to become an actor, you never get a reply. It's not that they are indifferent to your questions. Many of them, before entering the film industry, often asked the same question. They may really want to help you and tell you some secrets; but this is such a complex problem! Even if they wanted to tell you, they wouldn't have the energy. Where would they find the time?

Of course, Hollywood is full of people seeking work. Being able to get a job as an extra is already considered lucky; and to become a regular actor is indeed extremely difficult. But don't be discouraged. Opportunities are not non-existent, as long as you know how to enter the film industry. This doesn't mean going through back doors or seeking help from powerful people, but relying on your own efforts.

The question is very simple: "How can I get into the film industry?" But the answer is too complex. You need to know how to do makeup, how to read scripts, how to train your voice, how to practice your posture, how to correct unnatural and ungraceful aspects of your posture, and how to use gestures. You also need to know how much money to bring when you first come to Hollywood, how to live while waiting for opportunities, and so on. Of course, a star who doesn't know you can't possibly tell you all of this.

Now, that's great. A big star is willing to share her good experiences with you. She also climbed out of hardships and difficulties, so of course her words are very helpful to those who want to enter the film industry but have no way in. She is the famous blonde Kim Harlow. The following is her opinion:

"The first fundamental condition is that those who want to enter the film industry must first have the ability to cultivate themselves and fight against disappointment. Hollywood is an unpredictable and illusory place. Unless you have this steadfast and unyielding heart and indomitable ambition, you shouldn't come here. Because here, everything is uncertain. Today you get an opportunity that you think is guaranteed, but tomorrow it's snatched away by someone else."

"Any woman who wants to come to Hollywood to seek work should bring her own money to spend, and don't calculate in advance how much money she can earn in Hollywood. She should at least bring enough money to spend for a year. She must be able to afford her own fashionable clothes. This way, she will be financially independent and will have more opportunities. The cost of living in Hollywood is not very high. Rent and food are not too expensive. Clothes are the same all year round. A smart and calculating woman can get by in Hollywood for a year with one thousand two hundred U.S. dollars; if she can sacrifice some personal pleasures, she can even save some money."

"If you don't have a strong physique, you don't need to enter the film industry, because once you enter the film industry, the heavy workload can make you hunch over; even when you have nothing to do, that kind of unstable life can make it difficult for you to support yourself. So now the actresses in the film industry, if they are determined to move up, they dare not indulge in pleasure, they avoid alcohol and sex as if they were avoiding the plague, because the human body is not made of iron and stone, "burning a candle at both ends" is the most harmful. There is also one thing, a base reputation is the most undesirable. If you have a base reputation; you will lose good opportunities. When you come to Hollywood, you should cherish your reputation more than you do in your hometown." (To be continued)

Film Review

Review of "Strangers Return" 273

— Moore

"Strangers Return"

Originally, film criticism has become a formula. First, comment on the story, then add a review of the technique. Of course, for the convenience of writing, this is okay. But criticizing every film in this way is really too meaningless.

However, this film "Strangers Return" is first of all worthy of attention for its "story".

The "story" narrates "Old man Dole, prolific and ill, surrounded by his poor and greedy relatives, waiting for the old man to die so they can seize his fertile land. At this time, the old man's granddaughter Louise happens to return from the city. The old man spends his days wandering the fields. The girl meets the young man Clay and they fall in love. But Clay is a married man. The old man's relatives try their best to attack the girl, causing her to leave the old man; the old man is provoked and becomes mentally disturbed. The relatives think of secretly harming him, but the girl calms him down. His mind is clearer, and he writes his will and gives it to the girl before dying. And finally, Clay says goodbye to the girl and leaves his hometown to make a living in the city, because he doesn't want to burden the girl with love, and both sides move towards a bright future!"

We know that a "theme" becomes a theme after passing through the writer's consciousness, and there is a writer's creative method in action in between. Therefore, the writer's choice of subject matter, or the emphasis on a certain part of the subject matter, is the practice of the writer's creative method. The writer's views are determined by life. Therefore, old writers cannot easily see the reality of society, but excellent writers sometimes do see it. "Professor Tovey" is an excellent example. Now, although the central idea of this "Strangers Return" cannot escape from sympathizing with the old man with fertile land and hating the "petty" thinking of the "poor and greedy" relatives. But he is unable to deeply expose the internal nature of the property system, but in the end he has been able to jump out of the American film's happy ending of marriage between men and women, and make the two parties go their separate ways, which cannot be said to be progress.

"Strangers Return" is directed by King Vidor. Although King Vidor is not as familiar to the Chinese audience as Cecil B. DeMille and Ernst Lubitsch, he is not as unfamiliar as Pabst and Ingram, and his skills are as far above Lubitsch and others as Pabst and Ingram are. Like this "Strangers Return", he is able to use the literary description techniques of "Fleur-de-Lis" and "Madame Bovary" to narrate this "ordinary" (what naturalistic writers call "ordinary") story. Because there are no very dazzling plots in the story, like ordinary American films, the director also maintains a calm tone throughout. Even in scenes like the old man's death, he only makes the colors deep and not stimulating, which I think is very commendable.

Naturally, there are shortcomings, such as the lack of detailed expression of Clay's free and easy personality, so the final decisive action feels sudden.

As for the actors, Lionel Barrymore is very good, surpassing his other works, which may be due to the director's strength. Miriam Hopkins works hard.

The shots are also very good, especially the beauty of the outdoor scenes, of course, it is just the beauty sung by pastoral poets!

Audience Opinion

I Also Want to Review "Spring Tide" 274

— Zhi Qin

"Spring Tide" has been playing for a long time; I saw this film on the second day of its premiere. Originally, I wanted to write a review after seeing it, but I thought: this review is selling well, there are certain critics with special boxes, and besides, it's already the second day, so there's no hope of being quick, and if I send it in carelessly, I'll just be sending in a free ticket. But unexpectedly, there are still endless reviews in the newspaper now, and there are also a few reviewers whose names are unfamiliar. So I couldn't help but feel itchy, and wrote the following:

(1) Meaning: It is just a narrative of the sad romance of two infatuated men and women. Such a plain and boring story is something that we who have greater desires don't need to know. Even the song that Yu Ying groans when she is dying! "Sweet dreams, come back!" cannot win the tears of sympathy from the audience.

(2) Sound recording: It has the problem of incoherence. For example, when walking, in one environment, the leather shoes sometimes rustle, and sometimes there is no sound. In the ship, since it is a sound film, there is no sound of the ship's mechanical movement; In addition, the sound is blurred. Although I concentrate and listen quietly, I still can't understand what he is saying; but in other times, there are a few scenes that are unexpectedly clear; This new domestic sound film, this point makes me happy.

(3) Scenery; It's generally good, but it's inevitable that it's sometimes unrealistic.

(4) Actors; Gao Zhanfei performed very powerfully in the second half, but his expression at the beginning was lacking and a little dull. Wang Renmei's liveliness is her true color, but her sad expression in the second half is not very satisfactory. This is because the director did not carefully examine the distribution of characters. Li Li's portrayal of the harlot is so natural when she first appears on the screen, which is very rare. Yuan Congmei is still good, full of gentlemanly spirit, and the rest of the supporting roles are also competent.

(5) Cinematography; Several hours are very mature, only the opening scenes are vague.

Questions About "Small Toys" 275

— Wang Lianxiong

Yesterday I accidentally picked up the newspaper and saw such a large advertisement: it turned out that "Small Toys" was being re-screened at the Beijing Grand Theatre. I went to see it, and carefully chewed over the film I had just seen, and couldn't help but have the following questions; they are described below:

(1) When Yuan Pu and the wealthy woman were talking in the toy factory, it really made me confused and inexplicably baffled; when did Yuan Pu return to China? When did he open the toy factory? Although there are the words "only seven months after returning to China" in the subtitles, it does not explain the situation when he returned to China, and the ins and outs of opening the toy factory.

(2) Yuan Pu and the wealthy woman's acquaintance is also unclear.

(3) Who exactly is A Yong? How did he meet Zhu'er? How did he gradually become Zhu'er's lover? These are not adequately told to me on the screen either.

(4) When Aunt Ye heard the mantis dealer's story: After the news of her husband Lao Ye's sudden death, she immediately led her children 丨丨 Zhu'er and Yu'er to the place where Lao Ye died, in full view of the public, everyone saw that Yu'er was brought by her, so how could no one care when the kidnapper took Yu'er away? This also seems too unreasonable.

Silver Sea Talks

National Films Need to Emphasize Individual Performance 276

— Guang Yi

Pearl S. Buck, the author of "The Good Earth," once said: "We are all different, and whoever admits these differences and develops them as much as possible is wise."

From this we can know that if a person can develop his own unique differences, that is, his personality, to the greatest extent, his future has unlimited hope.

Let's look at foreign actors, they can all develop their unique personalities. They all have their special styles. For example, Emil Jannings, Adolphe Menjou, Chevalier, Chaplin, all of these people's works show their own unique differences. If their films were to be starred by someone else, and they tried to imitate the original star's actions as much as possible, I think the product would definitely not be as profound or moving as the original.

So I say that individual performance is easy to move the audience and give them a deep impression. If you only talk about imitating others, at best, you only imitate nine points; your success at most cannot be as successful as that person. Because that person is creative, and you are only imitating.

Are you saying that Marlene Dietrich is imitating Garbo? That's really a wrong idea. Marlene Dietrich's performance really has her own unique and strong personality, and she is even smarter than Garbo. I dare say that if she had completely imitated Garbo, she would not have achieved today's fame.

The unique differences of several comedic stars are even more obvious. The differences between Rock, Chaplin, and Buster Keaton are obvious, and I don't need to say more. If their performances were mutually plagiarized, then what value would we have?

Our country's film revival movement in recent years has created several products with some value. However, the content and performance often lack the development of personality and are instead imitating foreign products. This is really a bad phenomenon. For example, the situation when two people meet, the situation of parting, the situation of crying and laughing, and the situation of walking, are all often imitating imports. This makes the content of the work lack fullness. If I want to see your work that is being imitated as much as possible, I won't readily go directly to see the original product!

I don't want our country's stars to become Eastern Colmans, Eastern Laurel and Hardys, Eastern Clara Bows. I hope our silver screen produces more actors who emphasize personality, and hope that they can become world stars.

Five Hundred Professionals Elect Movie Actresses Joan Crawford Receives the Most Votes 277

— Xiao Lian

The American film magazine Screen play recently asked five hundred professionals to select an ideal woman from among the actresses.

These professionals included bankers, lawyers, doctors, journalists, and store clerks. They most welcomed Joan Crawford, Mae West, Jean Harlow, Ruby Keeler, Katharine Hepburn, Norma Shearer, and Ginger Rogers. The woman they idealize is a beautiful, moving, modern, and highly educated woman. They don't like someone as strong as Babe Didrickson, last year's Olympic all-around female track and field athlete, but they don't love skinny, sickly beauties either. They like women with feminine beauty, but they hope they are good companions.

Out of the five hundred people, everyone except one said that their ideal woman must have a good education, and all of them demanded that she must have a sense of humor. Few people describe their ideal woman as someone who can't swim, dance, play tennis, or golf. They want her to know a little about sports.

Half of the people said that she could smoke and drink, but not too much. Few people want his ideal character to be a social butterfly, but she should occupy a position in society.

Hollywood's Dog Hospital 278

— Fu

Because Hollywood stars are afraid of being too fat and damaging their appearance, they have to find ways to exercise and make themselves thinner. But now a new dog hospital has opened in Hollywood, and its special department is for treating dog obesity. It is said that if a dog is too fat, it will be bulky and not agile, which is unsightly; and it will lose exercise and easily get sick. If this kind of dog is sent to the hospital, it can lose weight and increase health without fasting. It is said that since the hospital opened, business has been very prosperous.

The Extravagant Feast of Movie Novels Is Hard to Repeat Dinner at Eight (3) 279

— Ma Teng

Laurel Renaud pondered... She was so beautifully dressed, so affectionate, so young... She was only nineteen, and he himself was nearly forty... Time passed so quickly that his rapid thoughts couldn't keep up. He did love her, no one had ever loved her like that. He had experienced too many women; he had been in love with women more than a hundred times. He had been married three times... To be honest, that third one still hasn't been properly divorced. How could Schiller love him again, that would only make her sad. He shouldn't repeat the mistakes of his life. Moreover, since he really loved her, he couldn't let her hurt himself again. He decided to awaken her fantasy to avoid a greater tragedy. He tried every means to tell her, but what was her answer? It was "I love you, Laurel; no matter what, I love you."

"You are young and inexperienced 丨" he held her jade hand and told her earnestly, "I'm all burned out. I only ask you to listen to me this time for the mistakes of my life." But before Laurel could finish speaking, Wheeler's lips were already pressed to his lips. Not letting him go on. She said, "I won't listen to you. I love you. No matter what you say, it's useless. I'm going to tell my parents 丨 and Ennis 丨 I'm going to tell them tonight." Laurel jumped up and shouted, "No 丨 you must not do that!"

The door creaked, telling them that a guest was coming. "That's Max," Laurel said, and went to open the door. Max was Laurel Renaud's agent. He must have brought good news, Laurel felt very excited; or a new contract to restore him to his former position in the film industry. Those fickle audiences, he must let them see that he hasn't finished yet! Schiller stared at him, expressing rebellion and deep love, and walked away silently.

Packard gasped and said, "No, no, I'm not going. Don't you remember what I told you last week?" Mrs. Packard said; "I don't remember! I can't remember what you said a minute ago!" Packard said: "Fool, didn't I tell you that I wanted to take over Jordan's company? Haha, that big fool is now delivering himself to my door, and he doesn't even know it! I'm going to that banquet. My new clothes will make their eyes pop out!" (To be continued)
